Fujian Government Borrowing Money from Xiamen Merchants 76

The Process of Chen, He, and Shen Going to Xiamen

Whether Lu Xingming is Alive or Dead is Still Difficult to Determine

Fuzhou Correspondence: Chen Peikun, He Gonggan, and Shen Qinmian went to Xiamen a few days ago to discuss borrowing money and reorganizing the salt affairs. Yesterday, the 21st, they suddenly returned to the province together. It is said that Chen originally intended to stay in Xiamen for a while, but he received a telegram from Chairman Yang urging him to return to the province due to the complexity of provincial affairs. Therefore, he only briefly communicated with various parties on the issue of salt surtax before leaving Xiamen to return to the province. He Gonggan met with representatives of the metal, seafood, and sugar taxes in Xiamen. He agreed to discuss the metal and sugar taxes at length, but he sternly rejected the request of Xiamen merchants to handle the seafood tax locally. As for how the borrowing of money went, there has been no news yet. Shen Qinmian's trip was to reorganize the salt affairs. On the 18th, he and Chen and He invited Wang Junxiu, the transport deputy, and advisors to the transport deputy office and directors of various salt affairs bureaus to hold a special meeting. Lin Guogeng, the commander of Xiamen, also attended. As a result, the income from the four downstream fields and the two bureaus in Xiamen was only more than 55,400 yuan per month. After allocating 38,000 yuan for the military expenses of Zhang Zhen's division, 25,000 yuan for the Xiamen Naval Command, and the expenses of the transport deputy office and various fields, the shortfall was resolved by merging the various fields in accordance with provincial regulations and reducing the assessment of various fields. Therefore, the expenses of the transport deputy office, various fields, bureau audit offices were reduced by a total of 8,800 yuan, which was still 4,000 yuan short, which was covered by the special finance office. Yang Shuzhuang led Lin Zhiyuan, Zheng Shijing, and five others to Nanjing a few days ago. In addition to reporting the experience of being detained by Lu Xingbang, Lin and others unanimously agreed on the matter of bailing out Lu Xingming. However, it is recently rumored here that Lu Xingming committed suicide by poisoning himself after being transferred to the Hangzhou Army Prison. The provincial government's personnel stationed in Shanghai also have the same report. However, it is believed here that Lu may not be willing to commit suicide, and there are other reasons. On the other hand, it is said that Yang Shuzhuang telegraphed the provincial government on the 20th, relaying Lu Xingbang's message that Xingming has been released by the Zhejiang government by order of Chairman Chiang. Lu's life and death issue is still difficult to predict for a while. (November 22nd)

Decline of Bandits and Communists in Various Districts of Chaozhou and Meizhou 77

Garrison Troops Launch Large-Scale Suppression Operations

Shantou Correspondence: The 62nd Division of the Garrison Troops in Chaozhou and Shantou, commanded by Xiang Hanping, has been ordered to suppress the communist bandits. The remnants of the 11th Army of the communist bandits in the upper and lower reaches of the Han River, led by Gu Dacun, have gradually been eliminated, and there are no large groups of communist bandits appearing. The situation is as follows:

Meixian Area: Huang Chengdian, the commander of the Special Service Battalion, sent troops to search for bandits in Luoyibao Angge, killing nine bandits and the rest fleeing to Nankeng. Li Siyi, the chairman of Jiuxiang who was attached to the bandits, and two local people Liu Limei and Liu Abing were captured. For several days, refugees from the bandit areas in Shunli, Da'ao, Xiaosu, and Shedu in the upper reaches of the Mei River have requested to surrender, numbering about a thousand. The organs of the bandit party have moved into Fengshun. Huang's battalion cooperated with the military police stationed at Matoushan to search the bandit nests in Huang Nili, Fengshun. They found the bandit party's puppet government and hospital organs. When the military police arrived, the bandit party fled into the deep mountains and forests. Two bandits were killed on the spot, and male bandit Yu Yashuang and female bandit Ruizhen were captured alive. Three seals of the Military Commission and the Red Guards and more than 20 small seals from various districts and villages were seized. Since the military police entered the area, more than 2,000 men and women have requested to surrender to the military police. Ma Yi, the commander of the Second Battalion, went to Jiulongzhang via Shuiche Xiaosang to suppress the bandits. He searched the bandit nests in Shiziling, Wanheshan, and Guaihushan, capturing 11 members of the bandit party and a seal of the puppet government of the Fifth Township of the Second District. Ma's battalion burned the jungles.

Fengshun Area: Kong Kequan's regiment has been suppressing the communist bandits for days. Guided by Zhu Dabang, a communist bandit who surrendered, they have captured dozens of people, including Li Pengji. Fifteen people were executed by shooting on the 11th. Kong's regiment commander and the county magistrate, in order to cut off the food supply of the communist bandits, dispatched military police to protect the people to cut the rice in the bandit area. On November 5, they first went to Dazhan, Yangweilong, Kengzili, Shangwuguo, Shanzixia, and Anzili to cut rice, with about 3,000 people attending. On the 6th, they went to Buxin to cut rice, with about 4,000 people participating. On the 7th, they went to Shankengwei, with about 5,000 people participating in the harvesting. On the 9th and 10th, the military police cooperated with 6,000 people to cut rice in the bandit areas of Yinyangao, Da'ao, and Shankengwei. They also unearthed countless rice grains stored by the communist bandits in Shihuangqi Jiaogongding. All the mountains and forests and houses where bandits could gather were set on fire. On the 13th, the military police cut all the rice fields in the bandit area and escorted them back to the county seat. From then on, the communist bandits had no food and could not stay in the mountains and forests for long.

Raoping and Dapu Areas: The people of Chishui Township in Dapu have awakened and risen up against the communists, requesting to surrender to the Gaobo Joint Defense Office, willing to serve as guides for suppressing the bandits. On the 11th, several hundred bandits gathered in Hecun. The county magistrate of Liang cooperated with Huang Chao's battalion to suppress them. From dawn to noon, the communist bandits were defeated and retreated to Xiashan. Dozens of bandits were killed and dozens of guns were captured in this battle. On the 14th, they began to return to the county. On the 15th, the bandits crossed the mountains of Shangxiashan and crossed Raoping Jiucun. The police team of Shangrao was weak and retreated, and Taoyuan Village and Raoping City were therefore under martial law.

Pingyuan Area: More than 1,000 communist bandits occupied Niudougang. The First Battalion of the Chen Ju Regiment stationed in Pingyuan cooperated with the Xunping police team to suppress them. When they arrived at Changchating Guanlaiba, they came into contact with more than 100 bandit sentries. The military police divided into three routes to encircle and advance. Five miles away from the market, a great battle took place and the bandits collapsed and retreated to Chetou. More than 10 bandits were killed on the spot. On the 14th, Niudougang was captured.

Puning Area: The instructor of the Jiaodao Regiment, Jin Ying, sent Yang Guoqiang's battalion to Guibei Village, Puning, to suppress the bandits. On the afternoon of the 9th, they met the 49th regiment of bandits outside the village. The bandit army, about 400 people, spoke Xiang and Yue dialects and were holding a meeting in the open space. Yang's battalion attacked the bandits, and after an hour of fierce fighting, the bandits were defeated and fled into the mountains on the left and right. Traces of blood were visible along the way, and 40 bandit corpses were left behind, one of whom was dressed as an officer. Luo Tuan telegraphed Shantou on the 10th to report the victory.

Hailufeng Area: The replenishment regiment reported by telegraph that its unit had destroyed the communist bandit organization in Baimanghua, Haifeng, killing 26 bandits and wounding dozens of others. Important documents and grain were captured. It was rumored that the bandits were holding a representative meeting of the three provinces of Min, Yue, and Gan, and were about to carry out violent riots in Zijing, Haifeng, and were coercing the villagers to join in providing food and supplies. After the bandits were defeated by Luo Tuan, most of them fled to Xianzhou, and a small number fled to Kenlai. (November 24th)

General Outline of the Four-Way Settlement Method 78

Xuzhou Correspondence: The conference on clearing vehicles on the Tianjin-Jiaoji, Longhai, and Pinghan Railways decided that the standard for clearing vehicles on each railway should be based on the military transport period from February 23 to November 15. The conference then announced the end of the conference. The situation has been recorded in previous letters. It is now known that the Tianjin-Longhai Railway will settle in Xuzhou. The settlement method will be determined by representatives of the two railways outside the conference. The Tianjin-Jiaoji Railway will settle in Jinan. The two parties have already decided on the method: (1) The Jiaoji and Jinpu Railways will submit a list of locomotives and vehicles that have passed through the Jinan Station. After the two parties have verified and signed without error, it will be used as the basis for clearing the handover. If there is a discrepancy in a part of the list between the two parties, the verified part will be processed first, and the rest will be verified by the Jiaoji and Jinpu Railways at Jinan Station based on the track transfer book before processing. (2) The original railway will send personnel to the factories and stations of the related railways to conduct on-site investigations together. If a locomotive or vehicle in the list of the previous item is found, the relationship railway bureau should be immediately notified and telegraphed for approval. The railway in charge nearby will be responsible for sending it to the connecting station and handle the handover of vehicles in accordance with the procedures. If it needs to pass through more than two railways, the middle railway will be responsible for transferring it so that the original railway can count the number of vehicles. If it is found that the locomotive or vehicle is occupied by the military, the relevant railway should telegraph the bureau to negotiate for its release and return to the original railway. (3) The personnel dispatched by the original railway should be given full assistance by the railway where they are located during the investigation period. (4) If there is any question, personnel from the directly related railways should be dispatched together to investigate the truth in the various sections and stations of the railway where they are located. The Longhai and Pinghan Railways will also decide on the method of settlement in Zhengzhou: (1) Each railway will send one person to settle in Zhengzhou. The Pinghan Railway will send Jin Zhongxun, the chief of the vehicle affairs study section, and the Longhai Railway will send Qing Xinjia, the chief of the vehicle affairs section. (2) The number of passenger vehicles, the number of freight vehicles, the tonnage, and the vehicle numbers recorded in the track transfer form signed by both parties will be cleared. (3) After the settlement is completed, the personnel dispatched by both parties should jointly make a report on the settlement results, sign it together, and each hold a copy to report to the railway bureau, and then each railway bureau will report it to the Ministry of Communications by telegram. (4) The railway that owes vehicles should return the difference in the comparison obtained from the settlement in full. If there are military personnel detained, the railway bureau where they are located should telegram the Ministry of Communications to find a way to negotiate for their release. Now that the representatives of each railway have returned to the railway to report, the Tianjin-Jiaoji Railway will settle in Jinan, and the Longhai and Pinghan Railways will also settle in Zhengzhou. However, the detailed settlement methods of the Tianjin-Longhai Railways still need to be negotiated. However, the disputes on the four railways can be resolved here.

Remnant Soldiers of Sun Dianying's Troop Dispersed 79

Cai Lizheng Handles Post-Disaster Relief

Bengbu Correspondence: The residents of Linbian and Baishan areas in the northwest of Suxian County, northern Anhui, were greatly ravaged by the remnant soldiers of Sun Dianying's troop. Just as the troops and militias of Suxian and Yongcheng were planning to advance together, the bandits in Cai Li and Suixi areas of Suxian were also suppressed by the Suxian Garrison and the People's Self-Defense Corps of each district. The bandit leaders Zhang Chuanwen, Wang Degong, Wang Kunlun, San Mao Hou, and Zhou Hanzi, seeing that the situation was not good, split into two groups and fled east and west. Those who fled east joined forces with Wang Xiaoting's bandits in the Jiagou area of the Tianjin-Pukou Railway and spread to the areas of Luding and Guigu. Those who fled west joined forces with Zhang Baoguo's remnant soldiers of Sun Dianying's troop, totaling about six or seven hundred men, more than 20 horses, and armed with more than 40 machine guns and hundreds of rifles. Soon after, a giant bandit Xiao Hongao led a group to join, totaling more than a thousand people, occupying the Li Kouji and Chen Laolou areas of Linbian and Baishan. A few days ago, the troops and militias of Suxian, Yongcheng, and Xiao counties pursued them from Cai Li. The fleeing soldiers and bandits also joined forces and fled westward, attempting to invade Yongcheng. They were intercepted head-on by the garrison troops stationed in Yongcheng. The fleeing soldiers and bandits then turned to the junction of Suxiao and Xiaoxian counties. The troops and militias of the three counties are still tracking and pursuing in order to annihilate them in the shortest possible time. The bandits in Cai Li and Suixi have been dispersed. The authorities have sent troops to garrison Cai Li and are now clearing the remaining bandits and handling local post-disaster relief. (27th)

Wuxi 84

Five Robberies Occurred in Xixiang: In the Xixiang 17th District (Fuan Township), at Shaotangying, the previous night, Gao Zhaosheng, a villager from near Xueyan Bridge, was returning home from the city by rented boat when he was suddenly shot and killed by robbers. On the same night, near the Qian She Bangkou in the same township, there was a rice boat from Yixing that had docked. Around 10 p.m., five or six robbers suddenly jumped down from the shore. They were all wearing tattered gray military uniforms, each armed with long guns, box cannons, and other fierce weapons. They overturned the cabin and thoroughly searched the boat, but fortunately, the rice on the boat had not yet been sold, so the losses were minimal. At about 11 p.m. that night, at a place less than a mile away from Shaotangying, the home of a tenant named Hu Aju was attacked by robbers who used huge stones to break down the door. They stole dozens of items of men's and women's clothing and more than ten silver dollars. The victim, Hu Aju, was also injured in the shoulders and back by the robbers' gun butts. Unexpectedly, at 12 p.m. that night, the robbers sneaked into Jingtingli, near that same place, and robbed the home of villager Zhang Awu, taking clothes, silver dollars, and other items totaling several hundred yuan. Before leaving, they shot and killed the owner's dog. The robbers, still unsatisfied after robbing Jingtingli, went to the Dabatou area of Qianqiao in the 4th District (Kaiyuan Township) with their guns and successively robbed the homes of villagers Xu Daen and Gu Laoer, looting more than ten silver dollars, 2,000 copper coins, and many items of clothing.

Using Mud and Copper Coins to Deceive and Obtain Goods: The other day, Ji Renyuan Hat and Shoe Store at Chong'an Temple, Tongyixing Umbrella Store outside Dongmen Tingzi Bridge, and a small foreign goods store at Jieguan Tingkou were all visited by a man who purchased shoes, umbrellas, foreign goods, etc. He placed what looked like thousands of copper coins and four or five packets of mud on the counter, claiming that he would take the goods to look at them and return shortly. He never came back. The stores opened the copper coins and discovered that they were mud, realizing that they had been deceived and were very upset. Furthermore, Wang Xiaolin, a resident of Houbeijie outside the North Gate, because his wife, Li, was not recovering from her illness, summoned a fortune teller, a certain Jia, to his home yesterday afternoon to calculate her horoscope. Jia saw that Li was wearing three gold rings on her hand and, believing that there was profit to be made, spoke nonsense, saying that the woman's annual fortune was bad and that she needed to ward off evil stars. Li believed him and asked him to ward them off. Jia ordered Li to take off the three gold rings and put them in a cigarette can, and instructed Li to light incense, light candles, and kowtow in worship. During this time, Jia took the opportunity to leave. Afterwards, Li opened the cigarette can and discovered that the three gold rings had disappeared without a trace.

On the evening of the 25th, the Zhao family in nearby Huangtang Bridge, who were also celebrating a wedding, were also robbed by bandits, resulting in significant losses. It was also reported that on the evening of the 21st, four other families in the area, including a certain Xing, were robbed. According to the victims, the robbers spoke in a local dialect and were local ruffians.

Jingjiang 87

Chief of the 5th Public Security Bureau Dismissed: Huang Weibang, the chief of the 5th Public Security Bureau of Xingang, was dismissed because he accepted bribes and privately released land traffickers. After the people complained, the provincial government repeatedly ordered the county government to investigate the case. Yesterday, the county government arrested Huang Weibang and Wei Sanguan, who was involved in the case, for interrogation. Wei Sanguan confessed that Huang received 80 yuan, but Huang flatly denied it. The investigating judge Liang, believing that he was highly suspicious, ordered him to be handed over to the County Public Security Bureau for custody. The current chief of the County Public Security Bureau has temporarily dismissed him and handed him over to the Inspectorate for custody. He has also appointed Inspector Liu Wanshi to act as his replacement.

Nantong 88

Methods for Converting Public Funds and Copper Coins into Silver Dollars: The public funds for education and charity in Nantong, which are deposited in pawnshops and money shops to generate interest, are substantial. In recent years, there have been many disputes over the conversion of copper coins into silver dollars. On the 27th, the county government invited representatives from all walks of life to the Real Estate Management Office to mediate. It was decided that the principal would be converted at 1,600 copper coins per silver dollar, and the unpaid interest for five years would be converted at 1,800 copper coins per silver dollar. The county case was thus resolved.

Registration of Land in the Huainan Salt Reclamation Area: The various salt reclamation companies in Huainan reported that the Department of Finance was organizing land registration, which would be limited to the end of the year. However, the salt reclamation area has always been under the jurisdiction of the salt yards, and its nature is different from ordinary civilian land. They have specifically requested the Department of Finance to determine whether the jurisdiction should be changed and reported for compliance. The County Chiefs are Preparing to Go to the Province for Questioning: The Provincial Security Department's Military Law Division is interrogating Yan, the former police captain of Nantong, who was previously reported. The plaintiff and all the county chiefs have been summoned for questioning. The county chiefs have collected evidence of Yan's corruption and lawlessness and will go to the province together at the beginning of next month.

Funding for Township Public Offices Guaranteed: The funding for township public offices throughout Nantong County has been decided by the County Administrative Meeting to be allocated from the real estate sales tax at a rate of six percent of the contract price, with two-thirds going to the brokers and one-third going to the township public offices. The county government has announced the implementation of this regulation.

Jiangyin 89

Household Survey Meeting: The county government convened a household survey meeting on the morning of the 26th and resolved the following important issues: (1) The Household Survey Office must complete this survey within one month. It was resolved that the survey must be completed within the time limit (the survey period is before December 15th, and the total number of male and female households must be reported within 20 days, and the forms must be prepared and sent to the county government by December 25th for forwarding). (1) It was resolved that the urban area survey should be completed within one day. (1) It was resolved that the expenses for the household survey should be set at 1,400 yuan, with a budget prepared and submitted to the province. Of this, 80 yuan will be retained by the county for office use, and the remaining 1,320 yuan will be distributed to the Bing and Ding districts for distribution (100 yuan per district in the Bing group and 84 yuan per district in the Ding group).

Meeting to Solicit Construction Bonds: The county government's Finance Bureau convened a meeting of district chiefs, local gentry, and merchants on the afternoon of the 26th to solicit subscriptions for construction bonds. The following resolutions were passed: (1) Half of the construction bonds will be solicited first, with subscriptions paid in three installments. The remaining half will be jointly requested by the county bureau to be reduced. (1) Method of distribution of half of the bonds: the urban area will be responsible for 30%, and the rural area will be responsible for 70%. The urban area will be assigned 9,000 yuan, and the rural area will be assigned 21,000 yuan. Each Bing district in the rural area should subscribe 2,000 yuan, and each Ding district should subscribe 1,000 yuan. Because five or six of the Bing districts are bandit areas, each will be reduced by 1,000 yuan. The remaining 2,000 yuan will still be borne by the urban area (30%) and the rural area (70%). The urban area will add 600 yuan, totaling 9,600 yuan. The rural area's 70% will be divided among the Ding districts, with each Ding district subscribing 1,300 yuan.

A Young Woman Commits Suicide Out of Shame After an Attempted Rape: Shi, the daughter-in-law of Chu Chenglang in Lihua Township, Third District, was 22 years old. Her husband went to Suzhou to sell ducks and had not returned. On the night of the 21st, Lu Fugen, a local hooligan, broke into her room late at night with the intention of committing rape and snatched Shi's cotton pants. On the 22nd, she committed suicide behind the Chucao Port Tearoom. After mediation, Lu Fugen paid ten yuan, with six yuan going to the Chucao Port for expenses and the remaining four yuan given to Shi as travel expenses. Someone laughed at her for getting four yuan for one night. Shi felt deeply ashamed and committed suicide at home yesterday. Lu Fugen, the culprit, had already heard the news and fled. Only his father, Ao Guan, was apprehended. Yesterday afternoon, he reported to the Third District Public Office. District Chief Xu was in the city on official business and, after receiving a telegram, immediately presented the case to the county magistrate and requested that a coroner be sent to investigate.

Yangzhou 90

Tragic Jealousy Incident: In Yangzhuang, Fanchuan Town, the county seat, a man named Yang Changhai married a woman from a neighboring village named Xiao Cuizi the other day (the 25th). Because the woman was somewhat beautiful, she had an affair with Wang Xiaowuzi, a local rogue. Wang's marriage proposal was unsuccessful. On the day the woman was married, he disguised himself as a sedan carrier and insisted on carrying the wedding sedan to Yang's house. When night fell, Wang sneaked into the room, pulled out a short knife, stabbed Yang in the lower part, and cut off the woman's nipple. When neighbors heard calls for help and came to the rescue, they saw that Yang and the woman had lost consciousness due to excessive bleeding. Wang, having achieved his goal, fled without a trace.

Qingjiang 91

Another Bandit Alarm Outside the City: On the evening of the 23rd, Cao Shizhi and his wife, Meng, were in their Caoshunxing Iron Shop on Hebei Street in Xiaoshuimen when two bandits suddenly entered and asked Cao Shizhi to buy an axe. Shizhi asked his four-year-old son, Da Heshang, to pass the message and turned to get an axe. The bandits, seeing that there was no one else around, grabbed Meng's son and threatened her with a pistol, ordering her not to make a sound. Meng resisted, and they grappled to the door of the shop. The bandits pushed Meng to the ground and then fled along Yilou Lane on the north side of Cao's opposite street. By the time the police and local security forces arrived to pursue them, the bandits had already escaped far away through a gap in the dike north of the bus station. The police are still searching for them.

The Police Chief Pursues Recovery of Food Expenses: Zhao Zhenhua, the chief of the Huaiyin Public Security Bureau, had deducted five corners from the salary of each police chief starting in March of this year for food expenses. Over the months, the total amount saved was over 300 yuan. Zhao has been accused of wrongdoing, dismissed from his post, and detained in the county government. The new director, Zhu Ying, appointed by the Department, will arrive in Huai soon to take over. The police chiefs are deeply afraid that the money will be lost during the transition between the old and new administrations, so they collectively demanded the recovery of the funds from Acting Director Zhang Shouqian on the 23rd. Zhang stated that the matter was handled by Zhao and that he was not involved. He requested instructions from the county government, which ordered the chiefs to submit a roster with the names and number of police chiefs.

Rugao 92

Daoist Zhu Arrested for the Second Time: Zhen Tao, a notorious bandit known as the Hun Tianhou (Chaos-the-Heavens Marquis), Daoist Zhu, has committed countless acts of arson, robbery, and murder. He was previously captured by the Danma Lake Security Corps, to the delight of the local people. However, he was released on the pretext of surrendering himself. After the county government learned of the bandit's cruel and heinous crimes, it ordered the Tenth District Public Office to deliver him within a specified time limit. He was recaptured on the 32nd and sent to the county for interrogation.

Letters

Letter from Nanhui County Junior High School 93

Dear Editor, I am writing in response to an article in the Local Communications section of your newspaper on November 27 entitled "(Strike at Nanhui County Middle School)," which is completely unfounded and lacks any factual basis. The tuition fees for the Normal School were determined by the Education Bureau during the registration period, and there were no problems with payment during registration. The so-called strike is even more baseless. This letter is specifically to request a correction.

Letter from Changyuan Pig Company, 16th Pier 94

Dear Editor, I am writing in response to a local communication from Rugao in your newspaper on the 28th of this month, which stated that Guo, the captain of the detective team dispatched by the Rugao County Government, had captured a notorious bandit named Li Zhongru at the Changyuan Pig Company in the 16th Pier. After investigation, there is no such person as Li Zhongru in our company. There is only a pig merchant named Ding Xiaolan's son, Ding Xiaofu, who was recently harassed by five or six unidentified hooligans who demanded money at the Yuebin Hotel. The district office escorted them to the Municipal Public Security Bureau, which transferred them to the local court for interrogation. We are afraid that the rumor is inaccurate and confusing to the public, so we specifically request that your newspaper publish this letter in the "Letters to the Editor" section to clarify the facts. Sincerely, Changyuan Pig Company

Central University Student Union Requests Increase in School Funding to 3 Million 95

Nanjing, 28th - The Central University Student Union, renamed the Autonomous Association in compliance with regulations, convened its Third Congress of Representatives, composed of representatives elected from each faculty. Ginling College Celebrates Its 15th Anniversary Today 99

Ginling Women's College in the capital was founded in the autumn of the 4th year of the Republic of China and has now been around for 15 years. At the beginning of the school year, there were eight faculty members and only nine students. Later, the number of students increased, and the original school buildings were no longer sufficient. Therefore, in the autumn of the 12th year, a new school building was built in Taogu near Qingliang Mountain, covering an area of more than 250 acres. The buildings were connected to the clouds and the atmosphere was rejuvenating. The equipment was greatly expanded, and the number of students increased sharply. In the autumn of the 17th year, the board of directors elected Dr. Wu Yifang to succeed the American Mrs. Deborah Duncan, who was also the first graduate of the school. From the 8th to the 19th year of the Republic of China, a total of 170 students graduated from the university. Their service locations (north to 　Ning, south to Yunnan, west to Sichuan) cover more than ten provinces. Most of them are engaged in education, accounting for 60%. Those who are engaged in specialized academic research at home and abroad account for about 14%. Last autumn, a physical education program was added and 30 students graduated this summer, and they were assigned to physical education instruction. According to recent statistics, the current students represent more than ten provinces, and the women's middle schools they represent are about 60 in number. There is a scene of lush prosperity. It is reported that the school board has been approved by the Ministry of Education to be registered. The registration procedures for the school itself can be completed soon. The school name will be changed to Ginling College of Arts and Sciences, which is still a university organization. All Coelges should be called colleges. The English name will remain Ginling College. It is learned that the school is scheduled to hold a 15th-anniversary entertainment party this Saturday evening and has sent out invitations to people from all walks of life to visit. The program is as follows: (1) English drama (2) Kun Opera (Sweeping Flowers) 3) Mandarin Drama (Old Flames, New Light). In addition, there are also copper piano ensembles, Pipa solos, and Chinese music ensembles.

Report on the General Education Experiment Area of the Jiangsu Righteous Education Office 100

The Jiangsu Provincial Office for Joint Preparations for Compulsory Education has designated Taiping Township in Zhenjiang as a general education experimental area, naming it Zhongling New Village. It is actively preparing for this project, leaving no stone unturned. Recently, a survey of the entire village has been completed, and the staff of the office has classified and compiled various statistical tables into a booklet, which can be used as a reference for managing the new village. The following is an excerpt from the survey results: (1) The entire village has a total of 246 households. (2) The entire village has a total of 2,154 mu and 8 fen of land, with self-cultivated land accounting for 77.97% and leased land accounting for 22.03%. (3) The entire village has a total population of 1,209 people. With 246 households, each household averages 8 mu and 7 fen. With a population of 1,204 people, each person averages 1 mu and 7 fen. (4) The entire village has a total of 210 school-age children (assuming ages 7 to 14), with 101 males and 109 females. (5) The entire village has 125 young people (assuming ages 15 to 20), with 66 males and 59 females. (6) Farmers account for 46% of the entire village's occupations. Agriculture is the main occupation and industry is the secondary occupation, accounting for 22.5%. Agriculture is the main occupation and commerce is the secondary occupation, accounting for 19.6%. The rest are engaged in other miscellaneous occupations. (7) The entire village's houses are 95.4% thatched, 3.3% tiled, and the rest are tiled and thatched houses. (8) An economic survey of the entire village shows that 2 households are well-off, 120 households are moderate, and 124 households are not well-off.

County Education Bureau Plans for Elementary School Academic and Art Competition 102

The Shanghai County Education Bureau has scheduled the academic and art competitions for elementary schools this semester, with the senior grades competing on December 14th and the junior grades on December 7th. This newspaper has reported on this matter. The bureau has now finalized the competition rules, which were approved by the bureau affairs meeting. Yesterday, the bureau sent separate letters to the schools for their reference. The original letter and rules are copied below:

"Respectfully, regarding the academic and art competition rules for elementary schools this semester, which have been decided by the bureau affairs meeting to be held separately for senior and junior grades on December 7th and 14th, respectively. We have specially prepared ten articles of competition rules for the senior grades and hereby submit them for your reference. We hope that the participating students will be led by their principals to attend on time. First Semester Senior Grades Academic and Art Competition Rules: (1) Competition subject: Mandarin speech; (2) Location: Shanghai Middle School Experimental Elementary School; (3) Date: December 14th; (4) Time: Gather at the County Education Bureau at 10:00 AM, latecomers will not be allowed to participate; (5) Speech time: 5 minutes per person, exceeding the time will be invalid; (6) Number of participants: 3 students per school; (7) Awards: (A) Top 5 individuals; (B) Group: Awarded to the school with the highest average score; (8) Lunch will be provided by the bureau; (9) Travel expenses: Limited to 4 people per school; (10) Judging: To be appointed by the bureau. Junior Grades Academic and Art Competition Rules: (1) Test subjects: Mandarin, Arithmetic, General Knowledge; (2) Assembly locations: Central, Qiangshu, Beiqiao, Zhuanqiao, Tangwan, Yuxiu, Sanlin, Chenxing elementary schools; (3) Date: December 7th; (4) Time: 10:00 AM to 1:00 PM, latecomers will not be allowed to participate. Mandarin: 40 minutes in the morning, General Knowledge: 30 minutes. Arithmetic: 60 minutes in the afternoon; (5) Lunch: The school at the assembly location will estimate the number of participants from each school and provide meals or snacks on their behalf; (6) Number of participants: All fourth-grade students; (7) Awards: Refer to the previous session's rules; (8) The list of participating students will be printed by the bureau, and each school will register in advance and submit it to the testers on December 7th."

Shanghai Art College Holds Double Commemorative Ceremony 103

Nineteenth Anniversary of Founding ``` New School Building Completion

Yesterday (the 28th), the Shanghai Art College held a ceremony to commemorate its 19th anniversary and the completion of its new school building. The details are as follows: Around 9:00 AM, representatives from the city party headquarters Fan Zhengbo and Xu Yefu, representatives from the municipal government's education bureau Zhang Meisun, representatives from the school board Cai Yuanpei, and guests such as Ge Gongzhen and Xu Zhimo arrived at the school one after another. The meeting began at 9:00 AM, with the school orchestra playing music and performing the ceremony. Then, Acting Principal Wang Yuanbo delivered an opening speech and reported on the school's history, saying, "Today is the 19th anniversary of our school and the completion of our new school building. We are honored to have guests from all walks of life attend and deliver speeches. From now on, our colleagues will work hard in the arts and live up to the expectations of everyone." Next, Ding _, the Director of General Affairs and Dean of Academic Affairs, delivered a speech, saying, "Human life has two kinds of needs: one is specificity, that is, the development of science, and the other is spirit, which relies on art. Both Kant and Spencer believed that education seeks the perfection of man. Now the government is supporting schools in science, and I hope that in the future, it will also support art schools so that they can cultivate artistic talents and achieve spiritual perfection." Next, Xu Yefu, the representative of the city party headquarters, delivered a speech, saying, "How many art colleges in Shanghai have a 19-year history? How many Chinese art talents have a 19-year history? It can be said that besides your school, there is none. This is worth commemorating. Art is pure and great. How many of the 400 million compatriots in our country understand art? Your school has a 19-year history in such an environment where it is not understood by the public. This is worth commemorating. Your school has a 19-year history, and you must not be satisfied with the achievements of these ten years and make progress every day. You should work harder in the future." Next, Zhang Meisun, the representative of the municipal government's education bureau, Cai Yuanpei, the representative of the school board, and guests Ge Gongzhen and Xu Zhimo gave speeches. Next, the professors and student representatives gave speeches. The bell rang at 12:00, and thousands of people attended the ceremony.

Four University Mandarin Debate Competition Jiaotong and Fudan Gain Finals Rights 104

Yesterday Fudan Defeated Jinan. The Four University Mandarin Speech Competition of Fudan, Jinan, Guanghua, and Jiaotong has changed from a speech competition to a debate competition this semester, adopting a knockout system. Jiaotong and Guanghua were in one group and held their competition a few days ago, with Jiaotong winning and gaining the right to the finals. It is now known that the group of Jinan and Fudan held their competition at 2:15 PM yesterday (the 28th) at Fudan. The chairman was Pan Gongzhan, and the judges were Chen Tingrui, Gao Yihan, Jiang Wenyu, and He Bingsong. The debate topic was (The existing universities in Shanghai should find ways to merge into a large-scale university). The Fudan representatives were students Peng Qixin, Chen _ Sheng, and He Dehe. The Jinan representatives were students Ma Xingqian, Zhao Fengqi, and Zhang Guoquan. The Fudan representatives spoke from the positive side of the topic, and the Jinan representatives spoke from the negative side. Both sides debated eloquently, like a river flowing, with sharp tongues and fierce arguments. The audience of over a thousand people applauded and laughed. As a result, although the three Jinan representatives' debates from theoretical and factual aspects were also admirable and praised as rare, they were slightly inferior to Fudan. Therefore, Fudan won.

This City's Supervisory Committee Urges All Comrades 124

Hoping Comrades Will Polish Their Moral Integrity and Character

To Cultivate Superior Personalities and Serve as Exemplars for the People

This city's Supervisory Committee held its 23rd regular meeting at 10:00 AM the day before yesterday (the 27th). Those present included Wang Yansong, Chen Xizeng, Deng Tongwei, Zhu Yingpeng, and Jiang Huaishu. The standing committee elected Wang Yansong as chairman and Chen Bai as recorder. Many important cases were decided and assigned separately. Furthermore, the standing committee proposed that in the past, members of our party have often been criticized by society for their inappropriate behavior. Since the central authorities have repeatedly issued warnings, and the Fourth Plenary Session has issued a solemn instruction, it seems appropriate for this committee to reiterate the intent and urge all comrades in the city to consider whether this is appropriate, and to submit a draft letter of advice to all comrades in the city for public decision. The resolution was passed, and it was decided that it should be published immediately to all district party branches, so that all comrades can take note and be inspired.

Letter of Advice to All Comrades in the City: The military campaign against the rebels has been completed. The central authorities, concerned about whether the life and principles of our party can be realized, see that everything depends on whether the party's work can be intensified and advanced in the future. Therefore, the Fourth Plenary Session was convened to plan the reorganization and reform of fundamental issues. Regarding party affairs, the first priority is to determine the restructuring of party organization in order to seek unified decision-making and guidance over party affairs, to strengthen its organization and enrich its power, and to effectively avoid the past situation of division of labor leading to decentralization, and the alienation caused by decentralization. Secondly, the targets and key points of party work are now defined, so as to deeply plant the party's foundation in various social undertakings and organizations, to enhance the people's use of the four powers and the development of various social undertakings, and to integrate the party's principles with the national education system, so as to guide the youth of the country, both male and female, on the path of the Three Principles of the People, and to earnestly promote, guide and supervise the local people to engage in local self-government, so as to plant the foundation of democratic government. All planning is thorough and sufficient to serve as the guideline for all comrades in the future. Furthermore, the session earnestly exhorted all party comrades to point out the past misunderstandings among comrades regarding the party, the party headquarters, and the people, to identify the true and unsound points, and to show the way to understanding and self-cultivation, so that all party comrades can each reflect on themselves and correct each other. The sincere and earnest words are sufficient to make comrades deeply alert and strive to act without disgracing themselves. Our party's mission to advocate for national revolution lies in thoroughly eliminating the remnants of the feudal system and implementing the construction of the Three Principles of the People created by the late Premier Sun, in order to achieve the freedom, equality, independence, and liberation of the Chinese nation and state. Establishing this goal as a forerunner for the people, we were able to gather virtuous, talented, and wise individuals to jointly face decades of hardship and create a foundation relying on the struggle and sacrifice of the martyrs. In the end, we were able to

destroy the feudal forces and unify the hearts of the people. This was no accident. However, in the two years since the completion of the Northern Expedition, rebellious warlords have multiplied, and the communist bandits and vagrants have wandered aimlessly. The foundation of national interest and people's welfare has not been firmly established to increase the people's faith in the party. Moreover, those who seek personal gain have even infiltrated this party and recklessly committed injustice, hiding as a scourge among the people, thereby causing the people to develop antagonism towards the party, which obstructs the progress of the national revolution. This is truly lamentable. The late Premier Sun said, "Everyone should aim to serve, not to seize." He also said, "Individuals have no freedom, only the party has freedom." This has long been upheld by all party comrades.

Comrades

join this party and engage in national revolution with firm belief

and noble aspirations. Having devoted themselves to this blue and white banner, they should even more diligently learn from each other's mistakes, strive to follow the example of the martyrs, and promote the spirit of sacrificing oneself to benefit the people. From beginning to end, everyone should strive to enrich their intelligence, talent, and character to become a model for society, and further contribute their intelligence, talent, and character to this party, so that our party can utilize the great power accumulated by the intelligence, talent, and character of all party members to accomplish the task of implementing the Three Principles of the People. In the past, those who sought opportunities for personal gain were deluded by the delusion of individualism or even used the party for personal gain. Their actions were dissolute and extravagant, deviating from the likes and dislikes of society and the people. Their character deteriorated to an unfathomable extent, causing the people to not only fail to respect them but also lose sympathy and regard them with disdain, as if they were a privileged class disliked by society. This false association extends to the entire party, distancing it from the people, losing the ability to unite, guide, and fight together. With such party members, the party's reputation is damaged day by day, the party's foundation cannot be consolidated, and the national revolution suffers immense damage. How dangerous it is! Now that these unworthy party members have been gradually eliminated, and the bad habits and malpractices will also be cleared away, our loyal comrades should at this time especially exert themselves to extricate themselves from past humiliation and resolve this great crisis, and revive the revolutionary nature of the party. The central authorities' exhortations to all party comrades, urging them to be loyal and strive forward, are particularly sincere and profound. Our comrades, recognizing the weight of their own responsibilities and positions, should have a genuine understanding and seek to devote themselves to the party. This committee bears the heavy responsibility entrusted by all comrades in the city, and its earnest hope for all comrades in the city is to advance together. It is believed that our party bears the great responsibility of the national revolution, and it relies on the contributions of comrades, whose intelligence and talent can be combined to form a great force. What is urgently needed is for comrades to cultivate their personalities in order to establish their achievements. Therefore, what is expected of comrades day and night lies in polishing their moral integrity and character. Since we are endowed with intelligence and talent, we must also have a noble and pure personality in order to be the cornerstone for the success of great undertakings. If all party comrades can fully use their special intelligence

and unique personalities to distinguish themselves, uphold the party's mission, be cautious and self-disciplined, diligent, courageous, loyal, and trustworthy, earnestly adhere to the principles, endure hardships more than others, abide by the law and serve the public, work diligently and responsibly, enlighten the people's wisdom, assist the people's rights, and show the spirit of sacrificing the small self to fulfill the greater self, then party members will surely be respected and admired by the people, and they will be worthy of being models for the people. The party will surely gain the greatest faith and support from the people, and all measures taken can be directed towards success. The central authorities' admonishments to our comrades are thorough and detailed, and there is no need for this committee to reiterate them. The reason for saying it again is that the comrades in this city have already demonstrated a long and valuable history of fighting for the revolution, and the city is located in a crucial position, where all eyes are focused. The party's revolutionary responsibility borne by our comrades is even heavier and greater. Their words and actions are always watched by the people and are related to the progress of the party's future. Our comrades should know that they must first correct themselves before they can lead others, and they should be even more cautious and fearful, constantly reflecting on themselves, examining themselves, striving for self-improvement, and constantly renewing themselves, maintaining a glorious history, and striving to be models for the people, so as not to disgrace the party's mission. The task of building a great cause is heavy and the road is long. Let us strive together with all comrades in the city. Shanghai Special Supervisory Committee of the Chinese Nationalist Party, November of the 19th year.

British Economic Survey Group 125

Arriving in Shanghai Tonight or Tomorrow Morning

Chairman Chiang Kai-shek Hosts Reception in Nanjing

The British Far East Economic Survey Group boarded the British shipping company's Rawalpindi mail ship in Kobe on the 27th to come to China. It is expected to arrive in Shanghai tonight or tomorrow morning. According to sources from the British Consulate General in Shanghai, the group is expected to arrive tomorrow morning. After a brief reception in Shanghai, they are scheduled to enter Nanjing on the 3rd of next month. On the 4th, they will meet with Foreign Minister Wang Zhengting and formally visit government dignitaries. At noon, there will be a banquet at the International Club of the capital. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek will host an afternoon tea reception. That evening, Foreign Minister Wang will host the group. On the 5th, they will visit Sun Yat-sen Mausoleum and attend a banquet hosted by Nanjing Mayor Wei Daoming at noon. In the afternoon, the British Consul General in Nanjing, Mr. Huthart, will host a tea party. They will also attend a dinner party hosted by Railway Minister Sun Ke and Industry and Commerce Minister Kong Xiangxi. They will return to Shanghai on the 7th.

Organization: The group departed from London on September 19th, passed through Shanghai on October 30th to Japan, and has now completed its inspection in Japan. The inspection date in China is approximately three months. The group's organization has a special cotton industry group, with representatives from both labor and capital participating. The group is an official body dispatched by the British government, and its expenses are 10,000 pounds provided by the British government. The expenses for the cotton industry group are separately funded by the Lancashire Cotton Corporation with 6,000 pounds. After inspecting various countries in the Far East for half a year, they will return to England, with an estimated self-funded cost of 16,000 pounds. The cost of receptions by various sectors is not included. The members of the group are all British industrial and commercial tycoons. The list is as follows: (1) Chairman Sir Tomson is the chairman of the British Cotton Industry Joint Executive Committee. (2) Sir Allen is the vice president of the Cooperative Wholesale Society and chairman of the Cooperative Congress Parliamentary Committee. (3) Morcom is a director of Lloyds Bank and chairman of the British Electrical Manufacturers Association. (4) Bell is the secretary of the United Textile Factory Workers' Association. (5) Crose. (6) Peel is a member of the Industrial Development Council. In addition to Chairman Tomson and Bell, the cotton industry group includes (1) Pechnerlev of the Yarn Factory Cooperative Association, (2) Dukesburg of the United Textile Factory Workers' Association, (3) Emmerson of the Dyeing Factory Association, (4) Green of the Padiham Manufacturing Factory Association, (5) Lace and Wild of the Weber Cotton Industry Employers' Association, a group of eleven people.

Mission: The group is an official commercial delegation dispatched by the British government. The British regard it as the most important survey group to depart for the Far East in history. Its mission is to investigate the current state of British commerce with China and Japan, and report to its government on what methods should be adopted to develop and promote British commerce. The cotton industry group will assist the economic survey group in investigating the state of the cotton goods industry and report on methods of revitalization. The main areas of inspection in China are Shanghai, Hankou, and North China to Manchuria. In South China, Guangzhou is the center. As for its motivation, although the current situation in China is unstable, its import trade is increasing year by year. Britain has not occupied an appropriate position in this progress, and it has generally deteriorated since 1913. According to the report of Peel, a special committee member of the British Overseas Commercial Development Association, in 1913, Britain accounted for 17% of China's total import trade. In 1929, it fell to 9%, while China's import trade doubled between 1923 and 1929. In contrast, US trade with China increased by 6% in 1913 and by 17% in 1929. Japan also increased by 20% to 26%. Germany's trade with China also doubled after the European War. Therefore, the main task of the British Far East Economic Survey Group is to advise the London government on remedial measures after returning to the country.

Opposition From Two Groups in the Voice of the British Survey Group Coming to China 126

Requesting Compatriots to Refuse Hospitality

The Overseas Chinese from the British and Dutch Colonies of Southeast Asia, who were expelled, organized the Support Association for the Promotion of National Diplomacy in Nanjing. The Shanghai community held an Aid Xiao Anti-Dutch General Assembly the other day. Three representatives, Liao Peizhi, Luo Ciqi, and Feng Hanyue, were specially sent to Shanghai to participate. Now that the British Far East Economic Survey Group will arrive in Shanghai during the day, the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, and the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, are preparing to receive the representatives who have suffered the devastation and abuse of British imperialism. They are extremely dissatisfied with this and have formulated a declaration. Together with Mr. Zhuo Wuchu, the executive of the Overseas Chinese Federation, they took a car to the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs in Fenglin Bridge yesterday afternoon. The director of the office, Chen Shiguang, and Liu Yunfang, were not there. Yan Zhaosheng received them. Next, they went to the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau. Director Pan was also not in the bureau. Xu Jisan and Mo Qiang received them. Zhao Jinqing, the director of the Industry and Commerce Visiting Bureau, personally received them. The representatives all lamented the tragic situation of overseas Chinese oppressed by British imperialism. Our country should not entertain the Economic Survey Group coming to China. In addition, the Shanghai Aid Xiao Anti-Dutch General Assembly also has a telegram. The full text is as follows:

Declaration of the Support Association: Imperialists have always used political, military, and economic methods to invade China. Everyone knows this. Recently, the newspapers have been clamoring that the British Far East Economic Survey Group will arrive in Shanghai. Our country's foreign affairs authorities have ordered the Shanghai Office to contact the Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau and the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce to welcome them sincerely. We, the Overseas Chinese who have been brutally abused and expelled by British imperialism,

are very saddened to hear this news. Perhaps all compatriots and comrades in the country are as saddened as we are. Because the people of the country have a thorough understanding of the British imperialists' stubborn and unchanging policy of invading China. The intention of this Far East Economic Survey Group to come to China is, to put it bluntly, to carry out an economic invasion. If Britain trades with our country in a sincere and friendly manner, we do not advocate closing the country and refuse to connect with the mutual benefits of international commerce. But the facts tell us the opposite. The British imperialist colony of Singapore was originally a free port where anyone could live and trade freely. Why did the Governor of the area, Clementi, order the dissolution of the Kuomintang, arrest party members, imprison them, and impose the most cruel punishment? He then expelled them from the country in accordance with the bandit conscription law, and openly and strictly prohibited the promotion of domestic goods and the repatriation of Chinese workers. As a result, our overseas Chinese workers and businesses have suffered great losses. The late Premier Sun told us (those nations which treat us equally are our friends; those nations which treat us unequally are our enemies). Whether Britain is an ally or an enemy of our country is clear based on the facts. From the above, the British treat our overseas Chinese compatriots in this way, yet they still want to come to China to investigate and develop their economic invasion. If we flatter and welcome such enemies, wouldn't we be betraying the late Premier Sun's legacy? In other words, we would be traitors to the Three Principles of the People. Furthermore, Mr. Hu Hanmin, the speaker of the Legislative Yuan, said in a speech at the Legislative Yuan (Relieve the Suffering of Overseas Chinese Compatriots and Overthrow Imperialism): Chamberlain admitted that the British have always been small businessmen. In fact, businessmen must also treat customers well in order to develop their own trade. However, if they bully customers and oppress them at will, even if the world is big, there will probably be no such businessmen who can do good business for a long time. With the most grief-stricken and sincere heart, we implore the patriotic compatriots of the revolutionary government, hoping that they will unanimously refuse the Far East Economic Survey Group of British imperialism, refuse to entertain them, and ask all newspapers not to publish their news for their publicity. In order to implement the late Premier Sun's revolutionary spirit towards foreign countries and to save the crisis of national economic decline, we can only swear to overthrow the British imperialists who treat us unequally and their lackeys. In the event that the Far East Economic Survey Group is quite sincere in seeking contact with the central business community, they should first remove the obstacles that undermine Sino-British friendship. Please ask them to immediately send a telegram to the London government to dismiss Clementi, the governor of Singapore, and cancel all unequal harsh regulations that oppress the Kuomintang and torture the overseas Chinese, and correct past mistakes with equality and mutual benefit as the basis. Only then will it be worthy of our welcome. The Support Association for the Promotion of National Diplomacy for Overseas Chinese Expelled from British and Dutch Colonies in Southeast Asia.

Anti-Dutch Association Telegram: Central Party Headquarters, National Government, Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and all newspapers, groups, institutions, and compatriots: British imperialism harbors the ambition of economic invasion, and has specially organized the Far East Economic Survey Group to come to China to investigate. Our country's backward production and economic depression are all due to the imperialists' investigation of the details of the domestic economy, harboring the ambition of invasion. On the one hand, they will manipulate and buy up raw materials, and on the other hand, they will import machinery and textiles as much as possible. The weaknesses of industry and commerce are all in the eyes of foreigners as a result of the investigation, which will give British imperialism the basis to implement its invasion. It is better to refuse severely than to allow them in. Emphasizing national goods under the guise of finding ways to make a living is actually losing the way to enrich the people and improve customs. Moreover, in recent years, British imperialists have not hesitated to humiliate, torture, and oppress overseas Chinese in British territories, as our country has been unified and construction is expected. The General Assembly has passed a resolution to reject the British Far East Economic Survey Group. It is hoped that the gentlemen of the party and the country and the entire Chinese people will unanimously reject and refuse to entertain them in order to prevent the ambition of British imperial economic invasion. It will be a great fortune for industry and commerce, and a great fortune for the future of our overseas Chinese. Shanghai Aid Xiao Anti-Dutch General Assembly respectfully submits.

Telegram Requesting Refusal to Publish News About the Java Ships 127

The Aid Xiao Anti-Dutch General Assembly sent a telegram stating: Shen Bao to Xiamen, Hong Kong, Shantou, and domestic and foreign newspapers: Ms. Xiao Xin'an, a teacher from our country, was tragically raped in turn by the Dutch first and second mates of the Zhivaderd, a ship of the Java Company, treating our Chinese people as if they were chickens and dogs. All those with national consciousness hate it to the core. Newspapers are the voice of the people, and all movements of acceptance and rejection concern the overall situation. We urgently record the case and report it. We express our admiration for those who have refused to publish, and we request those who have not refused to publish to accept our request. We sincerely and humbly request your kind acceptance. Shanghai Aid Xiao Anti-Dutch General Assembly respectfully requests.

National Calendar Settlement is Extremely Difficult to Change 128

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce received a telegram yesterday from the Qianyegonghui in Jiangyan Town, Taixian County, stating: The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, please note that the date of the end of the year for the national calendar is approaching. I humbly believe that your council's decision to set the day before the beginning of spring as the final settlement date shows that you are considering all aspects and sympathizing with the difficulties of the business community. However, it has recently been reported that it has not been approved by the Social Affairs Bureau, so the settlement period is again in question. The settlement is an important key in the business world. If it is not extremely difficult, why would we repeatedly request it? Moreover, this is the case everywhere, and it is not just a private opinion of a few people. Therefore, we send a special telegram to request that you please consider the business situation and maintain the original plan for the convenience of the public. The Chamber of Commerce immediately replied by telegram, stating that the Preparatory Committee of the Qianyegonghui in Jiangyan Town, Taixian County, has been informed of the Jing telegram. After investigating, our chamber has previously presented to the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau a proposal to change the date of the final settlement date to the day before the beginning of spring, as requested by various industry associations in this city, but the order was not approved and it was difficult to approve it. Promoting the national calendar is a policy that must be implemented. It is feared that maintaining the original plan will not be easy. It is hoped that you will engage in preparations and personally implement it for the public good.

The Silk and Satin Industry Complies with the National Calendar for Settlement 129

The Members' Meeting Decided to Implement It

The Silk and Satin Industry Association recently convened a members' meeting to discuss in detail the issue of the national calendar year-end settlement. All agreed that the national calendar settlement this year has long been ordered by the government and cannot be changed.

The industry has already complied with this directive and issued newspaper announcements and sent out notices to all. As there are only a few days left until the end of the year, most industries are also complying. The silk shops have a lot of credit and some are thousands of miles away, so they should be notified in advance so that they can prepare early and end on schedule. The association will publish in the Minshen News and the New Third Report to inform all customers, and print 40,000 notices to be distributed to each member. All silver and goods transactions must be cleared by the end of the national calendar year to prevent excuses for intentional delays due to habits. It was unanimously decided to hand this over to the Document Section to draft a notice, which is transcribed below: "To our customers, since we received the order from the National Government to promote the national calendar, we have already published a notice in the newspaper and sent out notices. Now we have received Instruction No. 3850 from the Executive Yuan regarding the fact that the national calendar year-end settlement cannot be changed, which has been forwarded to the provincial and municipal governments for inspection and implementation. As the date of the final settlement at the end of the year is approaching, all silver and goods transactions must be settled by the end of the national calendar year. We hope that all customers will strictly abide by government orders and comply. In addition to publishing a notice in the newspaper, we will also send a letter to inform you. We hope that you will investigate and follow suit. Sincerely wishing you peace and prosperity, the Shanghai Silk and Satin Industry Association."

If the year cannot be ended on schedule, it will inevitably lead to financial stagnation. It is also heard that various Shanghai money houses are vigorously advocating reducing travel loans to avoid danger. The current operating rate is almost 50% less than in previous years. This is the peak season for various industries in winter, but they are affected by this, and various businesses cannot operate fully, causing each industry to decline day by day.

Cooperative Training Institute Held Opening Ceremony Yesterday 131

Tong Xingbai Gives a Speech

The Shanghai Special City Party Department-sponsored Cooperative Business Instructor Training Institute has been preparing for over a month. The internal organization has now been completed. The opening ceremony was held yesterday, with a total of 50 people attending, including faculty, students, and guests. The meeting was chaired by Tong Xingbai, the director, and recorded by Zhong Weishi. First, the chairman delivered a speech, followed by speeches from faculty members Zhang Tinghao and Cheng Junqing, and guests such as Zhang Guowei, on the theory and plans of the cooperative business, all of which were brief and profound. The speeches were very long. The chairman's speech is summarized as follows: Comrades, the Cooperative Business Instructor Training Institute sponsored by the Municipal Party Department is holding its opening ceremony today. Why do we want to run this training institute? If we know this, we can see that the Municipal Party Department is paying great attention to the cooperative business and is eager to realize it. It is generally believed that the relationship between the cooperative movement and the party is the same as that of the national goods movement and the afforestation movement, which are both subsidiary tasks of the party. However, it is not known that the cooperative business is the core of the economic construction of the Three Principles of the People. Because the Three Principles of the People not only solve political and national problems, but also solve economic problems. However, solving economic problems not only passively eliminates economic shortcomings, but also actively implements economic construction. How is the economic construction of the Three Principles of the People? The Premier's legacy has clearly told us that the economic evolution of the world and society is nothing more than four principles: (1) Improvement of social industry (2) Public ownership of transportation and transportation (3) Direct taxation (4) Socialization of distribution, but we can analyze and summarize it, it can be said that the first two types are to seek the development of production, and the latter two types are to seek the equality of distribution. In other words, it is to solve the problem of production and distribution. From this, it can be seen that the central issue of economics is nothing more than production and distribution. Because the first two items require the improvement of social industry and the return of transportation and transportation organs to public ownership, which are all methods to promote production development. The third item is direct taxation, which is levied on the surplus of the capitalist class to compensate for the deficit, and is also a method of equal distribution. As for the fourth item, the socialization of distribution, it explains the organization of cooperation. On the surface, it seems to be focused on distribution, but in fact, cooperation can not only solve the problem of distribution, but also solve the problem of production. Because the distribution of cooperative enterprises is for production, and the production of cooperative enterprises is for distribution. If the cooperative business is successful, the economic construction of society will have a foundation. Therefore, of the above four types of economic evolution, the fourth type is the most important. Therefore, the Premier alone praised the fourth type of socialization of distribution (that is, the cooperative system) the most and praised it continuously. In the future, the primary task of our party's economic construction is to fully develop cooperative enterprises, so that parasitic classes and plundering classes in society are reduced. The evolution of society and the welfare of the people all depend on this. Although the revolution has not been thoroughly successful, the bad elements in the country have gradually been cleared. The establishment of the social and economic system and the construction of economic organizations are the goals of our party's efforts in the future. The significance of our establishment of the Cooperative Business Instructor Training Institute lies in this point. However, the theory of cooperation is profound, and there are very few talents with this knowledge. Even the comrades of this party who study this knowledge are not many. Therefore, on the one hand, we must encourage comrades to study earnestly to cultivate specialized talents, and on the other hand, we must ask you to take on the responsibility of publicity and guidance, so that the people will have a general understanding and concrete construction of the cooperative business. At the same time, I hope that you will treat the cooperative business as a lifelong belief after you have completed your studies, and earnestly carry it out at any time and in any place. You must not only regard it as a tool for individuals to seek employment. You must know that the cooperative doctrine is a part of the Principle of People's Livelihood. Practicing the cooperative doctrine is to practice the Three Principles of the People. This time, the opening of the institute has also been taken up by the comrades of the China Cooperative Society as faculty members. I am very grateful for this enthusiasm and perseverance. At the same time, all comrades should also deeply understand this meaning and strive to learn in order to live up to the expectations of the lecturers and the original intention of the opening of this institute.

Preferred Design for the Generalissimo Commemorative Tower 132

By Messrs. Fan Wenzhao and Zhao Shen

A Brief Description of the Design's Outline

Ever since the passing of the Generalissimo, the Central Government, in order to forever commemorate and eternally extol his imperishable legacy, planned to allocate 500,000 national currency to construct a Generalissimo Commemorative Tower in the mausoleum grounds. The Mausoleum Management Committee invited renowned architects, both Chinese and foreign, to submit designs. Several months have passed, and yesterday the committee began evaluating the submitted designs. The design by Messrs. Fan Wenzhao and Zhao Shen, renowned architects of this city, was selected as the top choice. A brief outline of their design is as follows:

I. Exterior Plan of the Commemorative Tower: The entire tower adopts a purely classical Chinese style, emphasizing solemnity and elegance. Its total height is 220 feet, divided into 15 stories with an octagonal floor plan. The tower's base is built on two levels of stone

platforms, evoking the grandeur of mountains. Each level of the stone platform is divided into two layers. Platforms are constructed on the third and fifteenth stories of the tower body to allow visitors to ascend and view the surroundings. The remaining stories are free from platforms, so those desiring a panoramic view can ascend directly to the top, widely disseminating the Three Principles of the People. The tower's apex is a delicately designed pavilion, topped with a crowning roof to enhance its majestic appearance. Surrounding the tower is a broad octagonal platform, with four smaller platforms further down to amplify the tower's imposing presence and provide viewing areas for visitors.

II. Interior Plan of the Commemorative Tower: The interior of the tower has several key features: (1) Each floor is equipped with two escalators located in the center of the tower, arranged in a continuous loop, wide enough to facilitate comfortable ascending and descending and prevent collisions. (2) The corridors around each floor are uninterrupted, providing visitors with ample space to read the full text of the Three Principles of the People without overcrowding or confinement. (3) A deep well is located in the middle of the escalators on each floor, allowing visitors to look directly down from the top, transmitting sound and color from above and below to enhance interest. (4) Each floor is engraved with the Three Principles of the People in a connected sequence from bottom to top, ensuring that the text is uninterrupted. The font size of each section will be varied according to the length of the text and the available wall space on each floor. Each floor will be engraved with one section, or the section with a longer text will be engraved on a floor with a wider wall area, regardless of sequence. (5) On each floor, above the

engraved text, twenty-four windows are opened to ensure ample light and air circulation. Protective stone panels are installed below to achieve perfection.

III. Plan for the Surroundings of the Commemorative Tower: As the tower must be situated on the north-south axis of the mausoleum, the entire site layout must be designed according to this axis. Therefore, the original ring road around the mausoleum should be reconstructed as the main route directly leading to the commemorative tower. At the point where the central axis intersects with the ring road, a wide plaza should be created to accommodate parking. At one end of the plaza, a large stone archway will serve as the main entrance to the commemorative tower. From there, a paved path will lead up the slope to the platform surrounding the tower. In addition to the paved path, a ring

road will be constructed around the mountain so that visitors who do not wish to use the paved path can drive to the rear of the tower from either end of the main road, where a parking lot will be established. A convenient path will also be constructed on the back of the mountain, directly connecting to the existing road behind the mountain. Small pavilions will be built on both sides of the tower for visitors to rest and

relax.

IV. Construction Materials for the Commemorative Tower: To symbolize a model for eternal durability, the tower will be constructed with robust and durable materials. The tower's frame will be entirely made of reinforced concrete. The exterior walls and roof will be made of aesthetically pleasing granite. The interior walls, where the text will be engraved, will be made of marble. Escalators, railings, and other components will also be made of marble to achieve magnificence. Except for the steel, which must still be imported, all other materials will be sourced domestically.
