Water Company Should be Responsible for Water Cutoff 139

Taxpayers Association Sends Letter to Company

The Chinese Taxpayers Association sent a letter to the Shanghai Waterworks Company yesterday, stating: "We have received numerous letters from users reporting that your company has issued notices of impending water cutoff. While investigating these reports, we received a letter from Dou Yaoji, stating that on November 21st, the Shanghai Waterworks Company sent a letter stating that they should submit the tax bill for 90 taels for the rent, doubling the six-percent water fee for Kailu Road and Yangshupu Road, for verification. Otherwise, the water would be cut off on November 30th. Dou Yaoji submitted the water bill for these two locations, along with the water bills for Edward Road and Longmen Road, which are also managed by them, and for convenience, in accordance with practice, sent the six-percent water fee (as the letter specified 'Chinese houses, six-percent water fee') on November 24th. However, the company returned the bill and water fee in full, with a note adding the amount of the water fee. The dispute over the water company's price increase has not yet been resolved, and the November 30th deadline for the water cutoff is fast approaching. If the company disregards everything and actually cuts off the water, causing various losses, including life and property, to our owners and tenants, the company should bear full responsibility. In addition to sending a letter to the company questioning them, we are submitting a detailed account of the situation. We hope you will investigate. We are also responding to a letter from a citizen, stating: 'We acknowledge receipt of your letter of November 27th. Your method of dealing with the natural and arbitrary price increase is very reasonable. If all members of the association followed your example, we would certainly be able to achieve the goal of canceling the price increase. It can serve as a model for the members of the association. As for the water cutoff, the Shanghai Chinese Ratepayers Association, as the highest organization representing all residents, will certainly strive to restore the situation by reasoning and adopting effective measures, so there is no need to worry. If the company actually cuts off the water, then all responsibility should be borne by the company, as the harm caused by the water cutoff will be even more tragic than the unfortunate incident of May 30, 1925.' We are responding to your letter. We hope you will investigate." (New Sound News Agency)

Joint Defense of Four Counties Outside Songkou 141

Blockade of Coastal Ports

Strict Prevention of Bandit Intrusion

Although the bandits outside Wusongkou have been severely suppressed and scattered, the nearby counties fear their return. Therefore, the four counties of Nantong, Haimen, Chongming, and Qidong jointly held a meeting in Chongming the day before yesterday to discuss joint land and water defense measures. The results of the discussion were to form guerrilla teams to be stationed at key points. Water defense will be handled by the major squadrons of the Fourth District of the Wusong Water Police, which will send shallow-water warships to patrol the sea. Furthermore, to strictly prevent bandit intrusion, all coastal ports and remote small ports will be blocked until the winter defense period has passed, at which point they will be reopened.

Record of Li Guoliang's Kidnapping 144

Five Bandits Suddenly Arrive on Zhejiang Road

Gaining Entry by Pretending to Deliver Gifts

Kidnapping the Owner and Leaving a Ransom Note

Villagers Untie Him After He Spits Out Cotton

Yesterday at 7:00 PM, Li Guoliang, the Yunnanese owner of the Xingli Tin Mining Company at No. 818, Lane 2, Tongchunfang, Zhejiang Road, was suddenly visited by five bandits who claimed to be delivering a gift. They then produced guns and

confined everyone in the shop to one room, while abducting Li and taking him away by car. The details are as follows:

Dinner in High Spirits: Li Guoliang, a 32-year-old Yunnanese, has been in Shanghai for many years, running the Xingli Tin Mining Company at No. 818, Lane 2, Tongchunfang, Zhejiang Road, and also engaging in other side businesses. His family also lives upstairs. The company employs an accountant named Shang, two partners, and a cook. Yesterday at 6:00 PM, Li Guoliang returned from work, and by 7:00 PM, he was having dinner in the living room with his concubine and the accountant, Shang.

Gaining Entry by Pretending to Deliver Gifts: While Li and others were feasting, they suddenly heard someone calling from the back door. When asked what they wanted, the person replied that they had a gift for the accountant, Mr. Shang. The cook, Li Chunshan, thinking someone had come to deliver a gift, hurriedly opened the back door. Unexpectedly, five burly men rushed in, some wearing black overcoats, others in military uniforms, with varying accents. They produced guns and told the cook, Li Chunshan, not to make a sound, or he would be killed.

The Cook Cannot Escape: Having entered the premises, the bandits were bound to enter the room. Li Guoliang, seeing the situation was not good, tried to remain calm and asked what was happening. The five bandits produced guns and held them to everyone's chests, preventing them from speaking. His concubine, seeing this, turned pale with fear and trembled. The bandits then forced the accountant and the concubine into a small room and locked the door. The cook, seeing that the bandits had not yet targeted the house, thought of escaping through the front door but was spotted by the bandits, who threatened him with a gun, so Li dared not move.

Leaving a Note and Taking the Victim: Li Guoliang saw that the bandits were not stealing anything and did not know their intention. He stood dumbfounded in the room, waiting for the bandits' orders. Before long, the five bandits dragged Li out the back door, while

leaving a note, instructing his family not to report to the police. The cook, Li Chunshan, also managed to follow them to the alley entrance. The bandits forced Li into a car and sped off northward. The cook did not know the car's license plate number and did not call for help, which was foolish.

The Police Are Investigating: After seeing his boss kidnapped, Li Chunshan stood dumbfounded at the alley entrance. After a while, the police patrol arrived, and Li reported the situation. Although the Chinese and Western detectives searched everywhere, they could not find the bandits' trail. Reporters went to Li's residence to investigate. According to the cook, Li Chunshan, a few days ago, a fellow townsman of the boss came to borrow money, and because his request could not be satisfied, he left disgruntled. There had been no other unusual occurrences before this. It is now learned that the police believe this case is quite bizarre and are determined to crack it and arrest the bandits as soon as possible.

Bandits Hire a Car: About an hour before the incident occurred last night, around 6:05 PM, two uninvited guests suddenly arrived at the Northern Automobile Company at No. 35 Da San Wu, Lao Bei Menkou, Minguo Road, in the Southern City. One was wearing a grayish-green suit, the other a blue cloth jacket and trousers. The man in the suit was carrying a leather bag, and he claimed his name was Zhou. He said he needed to hire a car to go to Lafayette Road, Lafayette Lane. The company's accountant immediately ordered the driver, Xu Chunjian (a local, 26 years old), to drive vehicle No. 12486 (municipal number 4299), a yellow

Chevrolet convertible, to take them there.

The Driver Recounts the Incident: The car traveled west along Minguo Road, entered Fangbang Road, and passed the Nanyang Bridge, arriving directly at Lafayette Road. When it reached Lafayette Lane, the car stopped. A man in a gray robe was already waiting at the lane entrance. Seeing the car arrive, he jumped into the car. The man in the suit immediately ordered the driver to drive to Shanzhong Road. The driver obeyed and drove straight to the newly built road near No. 43 Beishanzhong Road, where he was told to stop. The man in the suit then

pulled out a gun, forced the driver out of the car, and dragged him to a bamboo fence

in a dark place.

The Driver Cries for Help: At the same time, a bandit took out wads of麻 cotton from his pocket and first tied the driver's hands behind his back to the bamboo fence. Then, he used a section of bamboo tube about an inch or two long, wrapped in cotton wool, to tightly gag the driver's mouth like a horse's bit. The driver was unable to speak. About ten minutes later, three bandits got into the car and sped off eastward. Another quarter of an hour later, a villager happened to pass by. The driver struggled and managed to spit out the cotton wool. Then, he cried out loudly for help. The villager heard the sound and, after investigating, untied him.

Reporting to the Police and Tracking Down the Car: After being untied with the villager's help, the driver ran to the nearby Baojian Road Police Station to report. After hearing the news, the police station immediately dispatched a detective to investigate in detail. The detective then ordered the driver to return to the car dealership and be on standby for questioning. At the same time, he telephoned various police stations in the Public Concession and the Chinese area to alert them to intercept the car. However, at exactly 7:00 PM, a kidnapping occurred at Tongchunfang, Zhejiang Road. Although the car's license plate number was not observed at the time, it was suspected that it was the same car from the Northern Automobile Company. It was not until around 10:00 PM that the car was discovered on Avenue Petain.

Pan Sha Desperate to Find Son, Mistakenly Reunites Another's Flesh and Blood 145

If They are Your Own Children

Why Ask Their Age?

Pan Sha, a local resident of Qipulu Road in the Public Concession, had a son who was abducted by bandits last year. Sha searched everywhere but could not find him. Overwhelmed by longing for his son, he almost fell ill. Fortunately, he recovered after strenuous treatment. However, he still did not forget his son and

would scrutinize any child of a similar age he encountered outside, hoping to find his beloved son. Yesterday morning, Sha was walking on Ningwu Road on business when he suddenly saw a woman around thirty years old with rather ugly features walking forward with a boy and a girl. The girl was slightly older than the boy, and both were between five and six years old. Sha originally wanted to continue walking, but he followed them. Suddenly, he heard the woman say to the girl, "How old are you this year?" The girl replied, "I'm six years old this year." Hearing the words "six years old," Sha was immediately reminded of his own heartbreak because his kidnapped son

was also six years old. Then, he thought that if these two children were the woman's own, she wouldn't need to ask their age. He also felt that the woman looked fierce, and it was difficult to avoid other suspicions. Once his suspicions were aroused, he paid even closer attention to her actions. After walking several dozen more steps, they arrived at a fruit stall. The woman and the two children stopped. The woman took out two small foreign coins, bought several oranges, and gave them to the two children. Then, they continued forward, but her movements seemed rushed. At this point, Sha felt even more strange and followed closely behind. Near Tianbaoli in Haining Road, the woman realized that someone was following her, and her behavior became somewhat artificial. Sha took another step forward

and asked the woman what her relationship was to the two children. The woman replied that they were the children of a neighbor, whom she was taking for a walk. Then, she pretended to say to the two children, "I've recognized this place, you can go back now." Hearing this, Sha retorted to the woman, "The two children are young and ignorant, how can you let them go back alone? Since they are your neighbors, why don't you accompany them back?" The woman was speechless at this point, and as the number of onlookers gradually increased, she falsely claimed that she didn't recognize the way back, so she was letting the two children lead the way. At this time, Xu Bangda, a member of the security corps, stepped forward to question the woman, who was evasive. He then called the police, and the group was taken to the First Precinct of the Fourth District of the Public Security Bureau on Mongolia Road. After questioning by Director Yao, it was learned that the woman was Ren Yan, thirty-four years old, living at No. 6 Gongxing Road, Xiaocaichang, Baoshan Road. Because she didn't know the way, she was letting the two children lead the way. The rest of her testimony was evasive. The two children, Shi Sanbao, six years old, and Shi Didi, four years old, were both young and ignorant and made no statements. While the interrogation was in progress, Shi Zhang, the children's father, rushed to the police station, reporting that his children were lost. The police ordered him to identify Shi Sanbao and Shi Didi, who were indeed his lost children. The children were joyfully reunited with their father, and he burst into tears. Sha, witnessing this scene, also felt saddened and almost wept. However, Ren Yan, who had committed the crime of abduction, could no longer deny it and confessed to kidnapping the children. The director then ordered her to be sent to the Judicial Section for review.

Wu Wanliang Narrowly Escapes Murder 146

Brothers Attempt Parricide

Lecherous Wife Provokes Lover

Wu Wanliang, a salt-merchant from Yancheng, ekes out a living as a boatman. He has two brothers, Wan Kang and Wan Shun. Wanliang's wife, Chu, however, is restless in her marriage, and is involved with her cousin, Wang Dahui, carrying on a clandestine affair for three years. Although Wanliang knows about this, he lacks any evidence. On the fourth day of the tenth lunar month, Wang Dahui suddenly conspired with Wan Kang and Wan Shun. Each carrying sharp knives, quicklime, ropes, etc., they secretly planned to murder Wu Wanliang. Unfortunately, the plan was discovered and foiled before any deed could be done. Wanliang, now wary, took extra precautions. Around 7 p.m. the other night, Wanliang moored his boat in a secluded spot, ready to sleep. As he was preparing for bed, he noticed a flash of light in the cabin. He quietly crept back in and saw five men and women, each carrying a weapon. Wu Wanliang was shocked and jumped from the bed, shouting for help. The water patrol heard the commotion, came forward to rescue him, and arrested four of the assailants. During questioning, Wu Wanliang claimed that his brother Wan Kang, carrying a rope, had already escaped. His younger brother, Wan Shun, carried a bag of quicklime, while Wang Dahui wielded a sharp knife. All the weapons had been thrown into the Suzhou River. Furthermore, Wu claimed, the reason his brothers had plotted this heinous crime was to seize his land. His wife, Chu, was also involved, conspiring with her lover, Wang Dahui, to murder him. After verifying his statement, the patrol leader sent the assailants to the Judicial Section for review.

Eight Years of Cohabitation Abandoned in a Day, The Sister Refuses Support, What Will Happen to the Children?

Rent Dispute in Jiyi Lane 150

Increased Rent Followed by Cancellation of Conditions

Landlord Counter-Sues Tenants for Unpaid Rent

Tenants in Jiyi Lane on Shanxi Road, due to the landlord Yizun Company, whose manager, Ye Shantao, instructed its rental agent, the British firm Tonghe Yanghang, to increase the rent but then canceled the agreed-upon terms, hired lawyer Chen Tingrui to file a lawsuit with the Special District Local Court. The lawsuit sought confirmation that the established lease agreement was valid. Because Yizun Company had already sold the property in Jiyi Lane to Hexing Company, owned by Xi Qisun, the lawsuit also requested a ruling that Hexing Company be bound by the aforementioned agreement. It is found that there are a total of twenty-eight or nine households of tenants in Jiyi Lane, and a large portion of them, seventeen households including Mohuaxuan, have joined this lawsuit. The reasons for their lawsuit are roughly as follows: The rent for houses in Jiyi Lane was already extremely high. On June 1st of this year, the rental agent Tonghe Yanghang, leveraging British influence, announced to all tenants that they had one month to move out under the guise of renovation, otherwise their rent would be more than doubled. The tenants did not dare to contend with such power. Representatives elected by the tenants' joint association repeatedly appealed to Tonghe and eventually agreed to the rent increase conditions: city-facing houses would increase by 50%, while those inside the lane would increase by 30%, from August 1st of the nineteenth year to July 31st of the twenty-fourth year, with no further rent increases or renovations. In addition, if the property was sold within these five years, the new owner would also be bound by these conditions. Wanliyuan, Weixinyufeng, and Yongsanjia had already paid rent according to the new rent amount and notified the tenants, and the agreed-upon conditions were recorded in the lease agreement, which was stamped and signed by the tenants. However, on September 19th, a letter suddenly arrived stating that Yishenghang, Xinminxuanshe, Mohuaxuan, and Yicheng Silk Factory had failed to comply with the agreement and were attempting to overturn the previous agreement. However, upon investigation, Yisheng and Yizun Company had signed a separate lease agreement, Xinmin had already exceeded half of the rent increase, Mohuaxuan had no objections, and Yicheng voluntarily terminated the lease. Therefore, how could they use this as an excuse to cancel the agreement? Then, on November 6th, a lawyer representing Hexing Company suddenly sent a letter stating that the company had purchased the property in Jiyi Lane and that Yizun Company had stated that it had not entered into any agreement with the tenants and requested that all tenants move out. The first defendant has acted deceitfully and with cunning, with the sole intention of raising land prices. Therefore, it should be ruled that the first defendant confirms the validity of the lease agreement and that the second defendant is equally bound by the agreement, etc. Yesterday morning, Judge Xu Wenrong held a hearing to question each plaintiff, who were all present. Wang Zeceng, representing the plaintiffs, stated that after receiving the Tonghe notice, he sought help from Lu Shaotang, who had a close relationship with the landlord Ye Shantao. It was not until July 24th that they agreed on the rent increase conditions and established the lease contract. Later, because the contract lacked witnesses, it was rewritten on September 13th and sent to each household by Tonghe for stamping. However, Tonghe had not yet signed it when Tonghe sent a letter on September 19th declaring its cancellation and insisting on eviction. This morning, each tenant also received a letter from Xinghe Business Company, representing Hexing Company, also forcing tenants to move out. Then, lawyer Chen Tingrui recounted the occurrence of this case and the reasons for the lawsuit, stating that it was still unclear whether Yizun Company had actually sold the property. It is now heard that Yizun has counter-sued for unpaid rent, which is unreasonable. Because the tenants not only do not owe rent, but also wish to pay according to the new rent amount, the landlord has delayed collecting it, so the tenants have deposited the rent into the bank. He then submitted all relevant letters, contracts, rental receipts, and bank deposit slips for each tenant as evidence. Next, Lu Zhongliang, the lawyer representing the defendant Ye Shantao, stated that because the houses had been thirty-one years old, they urgently needed renovation, so the tenants were notified to move out. The tenants then sent Lu Shaotang to discuss the matter.

Willing to increase rent, please defer the renovation for five years. The defendant does not dare to bear this dangerous

Responsibility. Therefore, Tonghe signed a contract with the tenants, requiring the tenants not to move or transfer for five years. The tenants had different opinions, with some unwilling to bear this heavy responsibility and others choosing to terminate their leases. Tonghe, seeing that the tenants' actions were inconsistent, sent a letter canceling the agreement. The current lawsuit is not from all tenants. However, these seventeen households owe more than eight thousand taels of rent as of November, so a counterclaim is filed and a declaration of execution is requested. Next, Cai Lucheng, the lawyer representing Xi Qisun, stated that Hexing Company purchased the property from Yizun for one million one hundred thousand taels of silver. On October 20th, an initial deposit of one hundred and ten thousand taels of silver was paid, and the remaining amount was scheduled to be paid by November 20th. When the deposit was paid, there was no news of any dispute. Later, upon seeing the tenants' advertisements, Hexing inquired with Yizun, who stated that they had not entered into any agreement with the tenants and that renovations could be guaranteed without difficulty. Now Hexing has notified the tenants to move out before January 30th. Now it is further stated verbally that counterclaims must also be filed against the tenants. Judge Xu then reviewed each piece of evidence presented by the three parties and returned them separately. Because Hexing Company will also file a counterclaim, the judge ordered the case to be rescheduled

Page 16

for further hearing after the complaint has been presented.

Municipal Government Bulletin Confirms the Name "Qingning Temple" 154

The Qingning Temple area in Pudong had a Qingning Temple built in the Song Dynasty, and the area was named after the temple. Later, because the market there became increasingly prosperous, the area was renamed Qingning City with a homophonic name. Recently, the Municipal Land and Public Works Bureaus canceled the old city and township names. The area is part of the Luxing District, and it is inconvenient to retain the name Qingning City. Therefore, they jointly requested the Municipal Government to restore the old name of Qingning Temple to conform to the new system. After receiving the request, the Municipal Government considered that Qingning Temple had historical significance and a significant impact on local customs. It was approved to use the old name and announced it to the public.

The Municipal Government Bulletin is issued for the purpose of announcing that the Land and Public Works Bureaus jointly reported that the current Qingning Temple area in Pudong had a Qingning Temple built in the Song Dynasty, and the area was actually named after the temple. However, the custom is to call it Gaomiao, forgetting the origin of the temple. The Pudong Tanggong Rehabilitation Bureau, in order to develop the area and gradually make it a new city, named the area Qingning City with a homophonic name. The local people also have the name Qingning City in their minds. Because of its far-reaching intentions, the municipal map made by the Ministry of Land and the Ministry of Public Works' municipal ferries and Shangchuan Transportation Company also occasionally use the name Tian Qingning City. However, since the establishment of this municipal government, all existing city and township names have been canceled. This area is part of the Luxing District of this city and should be renamed to restore the name Qingning Temple. After discussions with the Ministry of Land, it is proposed to request the Municipal Government to announce it by decree to inform the public whether it is appropriate and respectfully submit a document for review and implementation. Accordingly, this Qingning Temple has historical significance and a significant impact on local customs. It should be allowed to follow its old name and still name the area Qingning Temple. In addition to instructions, a joint bulletin is issued to inform the public.

Patrolman Accidentally Kills Someone While Carrying a Gun 155

A Six-Year-Old Girl Dies in Vain

Guo Yuntian, from Anhui, is a patrolman with number 328 at the French Concession Police Department, whose family resides in the rear building of number 225 Taiside Lang Road. Guo went to work on the 27th at 7:00 PM while armed with a handgun and secretly went to his residence to rest. At that time, a woman surnamed Zuo, the wife of Zuo Benyuan (who works as a waiter at the Xindu Apartment on Ben'ai Duo Ya Road), who lived in the same small room as Guo, had never seen a handgun before. Seeing that Guo was wearing a handgun, she asked Guo to see it. Guo was in the process of taking out the handgun when, unexpectedly, the gun's firing mechanism activated. The bullet inside the gun suddenly flew out. At that time, Zuo's six-year-old daughter, Zuo Damaozi, was nearby. The bullet hit the girl's head, causing her to fall to the ground bleeding profusely. The child's mother and others took her to the Red Cross Hospital on Hague Road for treatment by bicycle. The patrolman, seeing that he had caused the accident, did not report to the police department. Instead, he took off his uniform and equipment and threw them over the police department's wall and fled without a trace. Although the girl was treated with all her strength by the doctors after being admitted to the hospital, the brain damage was too severe to cure. She died that night. Yesterday, the Criminal Section of the French Concession Police Department summoned the relatives of the deceased to the scene and reported to Judge Zhu of the French Public Concession Court, who came to the scene and confirmed that the girl died of a gunshot wound. He instructed the relatives of the deceased to collect the body themselves pending review.

Drivers Must Pay Attention to Hand Signals 158

The Traffic Section of the Public Concession Police Department yesterday issued a circular stating that the office usually provides drivers with hand signal diagrams and instructs them to follow them. When applying for a driver's license, the use of hand signals must be tested before a license is issued, because these hand signals are extremely important in avoiding accidents. However, the office has recently received reports from citizens that drivers are not giving hand signals. In the future, if citizens see drivers not giving hand signals when they should be given, and any violations of traffic regulations, regardless of the car owner or driver, they should report to the Traffic Section. Unless the circumstances are serious and require a criminal complaint, and the reporter is willing to appear in court to testify, the office will keep the reporter's name confidential. After receiving the report, the office will warn the car owner and driver according to the severity of the circumstances and record it in the driver's performance record for future reference. The use of hand signals and traffic regulations are attached below. Drivers are requested to pay special attention to reduce car accidents and avoid causing death or injury.

Public Concession Public Works Bureau Bulletin No. 4031 (Regarding the Amendment of Traffic Regulations) announces that Traffic Regulation 31 relates to the use of hand signals by vehicle drivers and has now been amended to include the following paragraph: "To give the above signals, they may alternately use a mechanical or electrical device of a type approved by the Chief of Police. The installation of this device must not protrude beyond the overall width of the vehicle." This is specially announced to the public. Edward, Chief Executive, November 20, 1930.

First, Committee Member Tao Yishan raised his right hand and read the oath. Then, Supervisor Lin Changfeng gave a speech, which mainly included three points: (1) Unite internally; (2) concentrate strength; (3) strive to improve knowledge in addition to work. Afterwards, Committee Member Tao Yishan replied, stating that he respectfully accepts the supervisor's instructions and will be loyal to his duties and not act emotionally. Finally, he reported on the recent situation of the Shanghai County Party Affairs Rectification work. The ceremony was adjourned.

Ham Industry Holds Citywide Representative Meeting Yesterday 162

Discussing the Hygiene Bureau's Collection of Inspection Fees

More than 80 companies in the city's ham industry held a citywide representative meeting yesterday because the industry association recently received a letter from the Municipal Finance Bureau stating: "The Hygiene Bureau's letter No. 2982 stated that the inspection before and after slaughter has been fully implemented for pigs, cattle, and sheep transported to the concession and slaughtered and sold in the city. It is also necessary to inspect meat products transported from other provinces or outside the city. The Bureau has drafted the "Management Regulations for Meat Products Entering the City Inspection" and submitted it to the Municipal Government for approval in Directive No. 7592 for promulgation. (Omitted in the middle) Your bureau should be in charge and it is hoped that you will consult with meat merchants directly and separately. Once preparations are complete

The Bureau will begin the inspection work (omitted below)." Another inspection rule is attached, which stipulates that an inspection fee of one yuan per hundred catties of silver dollars will be charged. Violators will be ordered to have their inspection at the place of origin and fined two yuan per hundred catties of silver dollars. After receiving this letter, the association considered that ham and cured meat is a product that has undergone sophisticated processing and is durable for long-term storage, which is different from fresh pork, beef, and mutton and does not require inspection. Now suddenly adding inspection fees is tantamount to harming merchants. Therefore, the citywide representative meeting unanimously decided to oppose it and submitted a petition to the municipal government to revoke this announcement to alleviate business difficulties.

Chinese and Foreign Factories Must Comply Equally

Since the National Government issued a clear order stipulating the factory commemoration and holiday method, most factories in the city have followed it. issued instructions to the Social Affairs Bureau yesterday to forward the instructions to all factories for compliance.

A Large Number of Gold Bars Found Inside Japanese Ship 165

Worth More Than 40,000 Silver Dollars

Yesterday, when the Shanghai Maru of the Japanese Mail Company was departing from Shanghai, Customs officers searched the ship while passengers were boarding at the Huishan Wharf. Free Talk

A Word of Insight 175

— Long

A person who can think clearly and see through things will feel happy even in adversity; otherwise, even in favorable circumstances, they will have many troubles.

Often, things that seem to be almost certain often change temporarily and lead to disappointment. Therefore, no matter what you do, avoid boasting before it succeeds.

Those who are good at using people employ both kindness and severity.

They can make both the wise and the foolish fulfill their duties and achieve practical results. Those who are not good at using people take improper measures and can make the wise feel like sitting on pins and needles and the foolish show anger, which leads to many troubles.

A woman cannot truly understand her partner until after marriage because no matter who a man and woman associate with, they will never reveal their true selves until they achieve their goal.

The love between husband and wife is prone to change midway, but only a loving mother's love for her children is always fervent.

Low grain prices are indeed a blessing for the poor, but the prices of goods that have risen due to high rice prices should also fall accordingly.

Patriotism and saving the country cannot be achieved by the verbal propaganda of a few people; it must start with the united efforts of people from all walks of life to resist foreign goods.

During the tense northwest wind, the physical suffering of the poor due to hunger and cold is certainly many times greater than that of the rich, but the mental suffering of the rich due to the surrounding thieves is also many times greater than that of the poor.

News of Chrysanthemums in the Old Capital 176

— Zui Ling

Yang Xiaolou returned to Beijing from Tianjin to perform three days of charity plays: (1) "Disturbing Heaven" (安天會), (2) "Farewell My Concubine" (别姬), (3) "Returning to Jingzhou" (回荆州), also playing Zhang Guilan in "𧈢蜡廟" in a cross-dressing role. Xiaolou's face is gaunt, and his coughing is more frequent. He is no longer as majestic as before. Tianjin newspapers reported that Xiaolou had accepted a contract from the Shanghai Grand Theater with a salary of 15,000, the same as Mei Lanfang. Shanghai newspapers, however, claimed that Xiaolou was actually coming to perform at a Chen family hall performance. In fact, neither is true. Xiaolou's actions are always decided by his son-in-law, Xiao Wutong. Xiao Wutong has already collected a deposit and will perform at the Kai Ming Theater, as seen in the posters, but the play list has not been determined.

Mei Lanfang arrived in Tianjin on the 24th for a one-day stay and then proceeded south because Meng Xiaodong was in Tianjin and they needed to say goodbye separately. There was talk of not bringing Wang Fengqing on this trip, but Wang Fengqing has already appeared on Shanghai posters, so he probably won't be abandoned in his old age. Recalling the early years of the Republic, Mei and Wang came to Shanghai together to perform at the Dan Gui First Stage. Fengqing's salary was 1,200, while Mei's was only 800. Recalling that year, Fengqing must have had the sigh of "someone's mother is old and no longer useful."

Ma Lianliang's performances in Tianjin clearly have excellent audience appeal, but every time he appears, there is a rebellion. New plays such as "Hongmen Banquet", "Chu-Han Contention", and "诛仙鎭" are about to be performed. In fact, "Chu-Han Contention" is "Burning Ji Xin," "诛仙鎭" is "Wang Zuo Cutting Off His Arm," and "Hongmen Banquet" seems to be "Rouge 折." Recently, Beijing actors have liked to arrange old plays and change their names, probably to attract audiences. For example, Yan Jupeng's recently arranged "The Biography of Loyalty and Filial Piety" is a combination of "Scolding Yang Guang" and "Nanyang Pass," or one might be puzzled when first seeing the posters, but one would suddenly understand as soon as one enters the theater.

Xun Huisheng and Shang Xiaoyun both have new plays. Xun's is "Legend of the White Snake", "The Woman Warrior of Eastern Wu," and Shang's is "Emei Sword", "Peach Blossom Formation". In terms of scriptwriting, Xun is better than Shang, but in terms of box office appeal, Shang is better than Xun.

Wang Youchen's performances in Shanghai are the most tepid, but his performances in Tianjin are unusually energetic. He likes to use the "嘎"調 and high-pitched singing, even surpassing Gao Qingkui. The people of Tianjin also value him more than Gao Ma, probably because the residual power of the son-in-law of Tan Xinpei is still present.

Gao Qingkui has a son named Sheng Lin who is studying at Fu Liancheng. His every move closely resembles Qingkui. Watching him, one almost suspects that Qingkui has been shrunk and is performing a puppet show on stage, which is extremely interesting. Fu Liancheng is a famous small troupe in Beijing. Tickets for each performance are sold out ten days in advance. Among them, Ye Shengzhang is the best. Ye is a disciple of Wang Changlin. The plays "巧連環", "盗甲祥梅寺", etc., that he performs are truly what the theater posters call "青出盖世, 　絕無上者也".

New Lyrics from the Cedar Garden

Tune: "Fairy of the Cave" - Xiling Sanitarium 177

— Tianxu Wosheng

North of Xiling Bridge, rising are exquisite pavilions and buildings, with six-pane glass windows facing the lake, as if heaven opens a painting. People are in a fairyland, just leaning against the mother-of-pearl stone. Qianjiao and Yu Huang mountains have good colors, and are just opposite the flying clouds and wavy reflections, wrinkled Luoxiu. The autumn water is as green as smoke. On the Willow Embankment, I am used to pulling painting boats to berth, making a neighbor of Su Xiaoxiao and Lin Bu. I wait to move my zither and wine pot, to accompany their plum blossoms and cranes.

How many generations of workers remember the past? Concealment of the seclusion is entangled with dust, suffering from the same disease. Let us steal a few days of leisure, take a rest, and come to drink wildly in the building outside the building, asking nothing about the rise and fall of the country. The Tang, Song, Yuan, and Ming dynasties all perish the same way, in the water reflection. Only two snow-capped peaks are free to come and go, regardless of the cold Xiling wind. I listen to several chimes of the morning bells, all from the forest, their traces are not yet ripe, and the yellow millet dream should urge them to wake up.

Tune: "Fairy of the Cave" - Xiling Sanitarium 178

— Xiao Cui

Green shade and drizzle set off the lake light, extending thousands of acres far away. The exquisite pagoda is thinner than bamboo shoots. The Zheng jade cup tries tea, really wrapping up the fragrance. Quietly, it is green to half the building. The mountain shadows are red, living near the water, the winding weeping willows absorb spring upside down. People enter the mandarin duck mirror. Taking a narrow-sleeved azure cloud with them, they load it on a short awning boat, and the pumpkin tendrils go to the clouds and waters to spend Qingming. There is mulberry leaf tea, and apricot blossoms stick.

Willow silk helps the peach blossom horse.

A Record of the City God Bestowing a Name and Seal Decree 180

— Juemi

The national government, in its efforts to eliminate folk superstitions, has repeatedly admonished in recent years, no less than three orders and five declarations. However, folk superstition cannot be eliminated, especially in my hometown. I have lived at home for four months and seen that when people in my village fall ill, their families must first ask a female witch to see ghosts, and then ask a Taoist priest to pray, believing that all illnesses are caused by ghosts or afflicted by evil stars. Therefore, when a patient first falls ill, one only hears the cries of joy from the family, the sounds of Taoist priests' gongs and drums, and all kinds of superstitious acts such as sending ghosts, offering plays to thank the gods, asking for blessings, borrowing longevity from the public, and making wishes. When all this has no effect, they begin to ask a doctor to treat them. Therefore, when they finally call a doctor and take medicine, the patient's illness has often entered the marrow and cannot be treated. There are many cases where it is too late for treatment. A certain Gong, who sets up ropes and indulges in Shanghai for business, is not bad at his age. A son born at the age of 14 is like Shang Qu who first gave birth at the age of forty. Therefore, Zhong Ai is very special. Last month, his son became ill, so he also asked a female witch to see ghosts and a Taoist priest to pray. After the Taoist priest repeatedly resolved the stars and sent out orders, and the female witch repeatedly summoned the dead and捣鬼, his son's illness actually seemed to disappear. However, hundreds of gold had been spent in these one or two months. His son has recovered, but he is still afraid of being infertile. The foolish people in my village, when they give birth to children who are repeatedly infertile, after giving birth to children, either entrust the name to Guanyin or entrust the name to Guan Yu, entrusting the protection of gods and Buddhas. Gong then entrusted his son's name to the City God Temple in Hongqiao. The City God's Mansion and the Guanyin Bodhisattva of the Shantang Temple specially sent two plates of steamed buns and cakes to the City God on that day, and offered a banquet in front of the City God with the Geng Tie, just like those who entrust their names in the human world. And the City God also bestowed a name like the human world and issued a seal decree to Gong for collection. The decree said: "Regarding the matter of giving the seal decree, according to the report of citizen Gong Heyun, he secretly stated that the only son, Lingjiang, born at the age of 55, is only fourteen years old. In recent years, his fate has been fraught with disasters. He secretly thinks that the Gong family relies on this one son to inherit. Unexpectedly, the evil stars are multiplying and the demons of illness are following closely, which is deeply worrying. Therefore, he made a submission to the钧府, begging for permission to entrust the name, relying on Weiling to silently protect, etc. According to this thought, Gong Heyun loves his son sincerely and the ancestral temple is important, so he is allowed to entrust the name, bestowing the name Yongbao. From now on, your son will see this government as a father, and this government will see your son as a son. With the protection of this government, he will forever eliminate disasters and difficulties, and ensure that he is free from disease and pain. In the future, he will be intelligent and will surely become a son who crosses the stove, inheriting the cause. This government has high hopes." This decree, etc., is usually done by the abbot of the temple, but the abbot cannot write, so someone is asked to write it, which is really laughable.

Interesting Scraps in the Car 181

— Zuichi Sheng

On the morning of the other day, I went to Dingjia Village in Malu Township for a diagnosis, first taking the Beijing-Shanghai train to Nanxiang. During this one-hour train ride, I heard and witnessed many interesting scraps, which I will recount as follows:

It's hard for the villagers: The person sitting next to me was a villager in short clothes and rough clothes. Later, the villager suddenly stood up, and the seat was suddenly occupied by a certain Jia, and a clothing bag was placed next to it. The villager reasoned with him, but Jia scolded the villager. The villager had to stand there like a wooden chicken. Before long, a woman came slowly, looking for a seat. Jia hurriedly packed up his clothing bag and let the woman sit down. The onlookers laughed secretly. I said that all unfair things in the world should be viewed in this way.

Cigarette butt as a farewell gift: The people sitting opposite me were a couple, whispering sweet nothings to each other. The man was over forty, and the woman was also middle-aged, but still charming. The Wu dialect was so soft that it made people's hearts melt. When the car was about to start, the man hurriedly got off the car, reluctant to leave. He leaned out the window and said goodbye to the woman earnestly, his attitude indescribable. Then the car started. The woman threw the cigarette butt from her cherry lips to him remotely. The man picked it up and smoked it, its taste as sweet as can be. These old folks still have such heroic and unrestrained ambitions in crowded places, not afraid of being 肉麻. I can only repeatedly call out my admiration and surrender.

Suffering from smoke and fire: I have never smoked cigarettes in my life, but at that time, I was sitting bored in the carriage, as if I were a vast leader suffering from smoke and fire. Unfortunately, I am not blessed enough to enjoy it. The surrounding smoke and dust were overwhelming, making people cough and choke constantly. The people of our country have such a fondness for it. Don't they think that every wisp of smoke is transformed from countless amounts of money?

An old scholar sings a song to awaken the world: At that time, a song suddenly arose from one corner. The crowd looked at it and saw a person who looked like a scholar was writing a book and singing a mountain song to persuade the world. There was a sentence in it: "Putting Coptis chinensis on the tip of the nose is bitter in front of the eyes, hanging licorice on the back is sweet later." It is both interesting and thought-provoking. I said that this kind of slang song is the easiest to popularize, more beneficial than the "drizzling rain" and "Jiang Lao Wu" sung from house to house.

Buying a third-class ticket and taking a fifth-class car: At half past two in the afternoon, I took a car from Nanxiang back to Shanghai. The people getting on the car were extremely crowded. I climbed onto a car that looked like a freight car. The men, women, old, and young were planted full, filling every pit and valley. The crowd complained that buying a third-class ticket and taking such a car was really not worth it. I said that this can be called a fifth-class car because fourth-class cars still have seats, but this one has no seats at all. Why is it not a fifth-class car? However, everyone is treated equally and stands, so as to avoid competing for seats. Therefore, it can also be called an equal car. The crowd smiled and the complaints gradually subsided.

Travel Notes from the South Seas (86) 182

— Linghua

The garden hangs a sign saying that tourists must not scare animals, otherwise they will be expelled. At the deer fence, two male deer are playing by butting each other's horns, while the doe roams leisurely. Seeing people coming, she greets them with her nose. It can be said that they are truly of the same group. No wonder the great舜 lived deep in the mountains and made friends with them, cultivating the saintly rule of禪讓. As for the male deer, they have nothing to do but enjoy fighting, while the antlerless female proves that the nature of a female is not to fight. My university is in animal society. I have long been a friend of the fawn at the Taiyuan Museum, so I feel this deeply and sigh that human morality is far inferior to that of birds and beasts. Therefore, I composed a poem. I have not met for a long time, but I now see Shun's friend. His innocence is truly brilliant, and he affectionately licks people's hands. His life is smooth and natural, and he cries to his mate. With few desires, he is easy to be content, and how can he have a scheming heart? A vegetarian is of good nature, and I feel that your face is kind.

Several does use their noses to nuzzle people. I then gave them green grass, and they slowly ate it. I then remembered that Master Wanhui also very much agreed with my theory that "humans are inferior to birds," saying that "the greatest evil in the world is none other than humans, and the most sinful of humans are the males who love to kill." This is Master Wanhui's judgment. I thought that the deer are so affectionate to people, but how can they know that humans have no good intentions towards all animals? Isn't it true that all horses, cattle, sheep, chickens, and dogs,凡near people, are all eaten for their meat and slept in their skin? Monkeys are very different. There are red-faced monkeys that are very similar to Sun Wukong with double pupils in the painting. There are also black pig monkeys that are very ugly. Generally, those who raise monkeys separate the males and females. The architecture of this garden is very large, with rooms above to avoid rain and iron barriers inside to divide them into multiple layers so that the monkeys can jump. In the past, I have seen many monkeys in the Beijing Zoo, and they are all made to jump on poles while wearing iron chains. When asked, the guard replied that it is inconvenient for these creatures, male and female, to gather in one place. Because of their lewd nature, they will often mate, which is unseemly for male and female tourists to see. From this, I can infer that the monkeys here must also be separated by male and female. Although, since Darwin, anthropologists must base their studies on animal society, especially the relationship between monkeys, apes, and society. Today, the principle of great equality between the sexes in our world is also based on animal sociology. In the past, someone in the education community said to me that if the education community wants to study psychology, it must first set up a monkey village and a children's village academy as the foundation for studying society and psychology. I think this plan should be considered by scholars all over the world, but

it is the foundation for studying humans, but the world rarely knows it.

Warmth in My Heart (324) 183

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter Sixteen: Cui Xiu Tirelessly Asks for Words From Her Teacher, Chivalrous Heroines Talk About Military Affairs at a Brothel Feast

Time is something that no amount of force can stop. Gradually, it has turned from early winter to deep winter. However, the weather in the south, even in the dead of winter, is unpredictable. Sometimes, even after the winter solstice, it suddenly becomes as warm as early spring. But after the warmth, it suddenly changes, and freezing clouds gather, suddenly becoming snow-brewing weather, and it snows all day long. The preparations for winter in the south are not as good as in the north. In the north, almost every house has a stove in the winter, with thick door curtains hanging, and all the windows and doors are pasted up, not allowing a single wisp of wind to enter. Large-scale residences and hotels have long had steam pipes running throughout the room. At that time in Shanghai, only a few large foreign companies had this scale. All the large hotels enjoyed by the Chinese did not have steam pipes yet. Ordinary people had not even seen them. Even the stoves were not in every household. Only a group of Cantonese people had just arrived in Shanghai. They had always lived in the southern temperate zone. In the winter, they shivered like 煨　cats, wanting to get close to the stove. Many people in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces cannot stand the stove. After roasting in the stove, tomorrow they will have a sore throat and toothache. Only a few friends wearing suits must have a stove. Although their winter clothes are exquisite, they cannot compare to the warmth of Chinese clothes, especially on the lower body, with only a pair of single pants worn on a pair of legs, the same single pants in summer and the same single pants in winter, but the quality is different. The editorial department of the Ping Bao Pavilion also installed a stove. This was for the group of people in suits like Liu Xing-shu. Now that the number of people wearing suits is gradually decreasing, several gentlemen do not need the stove very much, unless it is after late at night that they teach the waiter to light the stove. However, there are several people wearing suits who often come to play at the Ping Bao Pavilion. Among them, there is one named Ye, called Ye Haoran. He is a graduate of Japan. He is short and capable, but he is wise and resourceful. He originally studied commerce in Japan and received a bachelor's degree in commerce. After returning to China, he wanted to be active in domestic commerce, but he often went to the Ping Bao Pavilion with people like Ling Zhixiang and Long Ziyun. When it comes to eating dinner, he is also a newly joined member. Moreover, he often makes a fuss about treating guests. Before departing, he must make an appointment with a group of people in advance, saying that today's host is me, and everyone should not搶. If it is once or twice, everyone agrees to disturb him. If the number of times he treats guests increases, everyone says that we cannot disturb you alone. Let's take turns treating. When they arrive at some restaurant, he is still very powerful. He orders, and after he audits the bill, others cannot pay it.

Depressed State of Both Chinese and Foreign Cloth Goods 206

The cloth market of our factory has trended loose again. Fine cloth has fallen by two and a half points, and coarse twill by a small five points. The formerly out-of-stock nine-pound coarse cloth has also gradually increased in quantity. Dragon and Five Bats are both quoted at four taels, three mace, and two and a half fen. Goods from Hubei arrive in increasing quantities daily, with "Tian" brand opening at eight taels and seven mace, "Horse Race" brand at eight taels and one and a half mace, and "Lu" brand at seven taels and seven and a half mace. Northern merchants have slightly purchased, but fine twill has a strong downward trend. The reason for this is the impact of year-end account settlements for the traditional Chinese calendar year. There is little hope for transactions within the year, so those holding goods are very apprehensive. Observation suggests that it will be difficult to reverse the downward trend in the short term.

Due to the warmer weather, the daily sales of Eastern fabrics have been sluggish, greatly affecting the business of stores. Therefore, velvet and other Eastern goods have started to fall again. "Wind and Waves" velvet continued to soften yesterday, with black flower continuing to be uniform, a small drop of one mace and eight and a half fen, and large flowers all selling for one mace and nine and a half fen. The upward trend of colored striped velvet has also stopped, with "Divine Arrow Yang Guifei" both opening at six taels and seven and a half mace. Only double-width thick camel velvet remains firm, with "Ming Fu Lu Shou" opening at eight mace and five fen. Sichuan merchants have purchased quite a bit of old-fashioned tribute broadcloth. Transactions in this street are quite active, with fifty or sixty pieces being sold. The price of bald red is three mace and two and a half fen, and colored tribute broadcloth has not stopped falling and has returned to two mace and two or three fen. The current transactions of Western goods are very pessimistic. Thick tribute broadcloth, Western satin, and yuan silk arrive in small quantities and are not selling well.

Rising Market for Hardware American Tinplate 207

Previously, the market for American tinplate was quiet, and arrivals surged, with stockpiles sufficient for several months of sales. In recent days, because the company's iron has reached its peak price, customers mostly buy American tinplate because of the high price. Therefore, the market is as active as that for eighteen-sheet black iron. However, after several rounds of procurement, the supply of goods has become scarce, and standards are rising steadily. The current price of ninety-pound iron is fourteen taels and eight and a half mace, more than four mace higher than before, and one hundred pounds is sixteen taels, also two mace and a half higher than before. It is said that egg factories, tobacco companies, canning factories, etc., have all been buying and selling for several days. The market has opened up to 1,800 or 1,900 boxes in the past three or four days, so the market is quite optimistic.

Shanghai Market

Commercial News 209

The Dahua National Products Woolen Factory announced that its manager, Mr. Gu Jiuru, has spared no effort in recent years to improve and imitate woolen fabrics, achieving special results in his products. Not only are sales widespread, but business has also increased rapidly. Now that winter is approaching, in order to promote the factory's excellent achievements and attract the attention of the Chinese people, it has been specifically scheduled for today and tomorrow to hold a national woolen fabric winter exhibition in the auditorium of the National Products Department Store on Nanjing Road. In addition to displaying the factory's various products, the factory has invited the Youth Propaganda Group, various dance troupes, and famous comedians Wang, Neng, Jiang Xiaoxiao, and Liu Chunshan to perform and entertain. Dozens of famous Shanghai beauties will also participate in the exhibition of the factory's various new and unique winter woolen fabrics.

The Daxin Silk and Satin Bureau on Sanma Road, Shilu, is holding a three-week winter sale starting today, collecting thousands of kinds of famous silk and satin fabrics, with genuine markdowns. Among them, the Electric Factory crepe, Maozhen crepe, Kirin crepe, and patterned soft satin are all made of high-quality silk and are very suitable for making winter clothing. They are indeed excellent seasonal products.

The Qihua Department Store opposite Hongmiao on Nanjing Road announced that in order to reward its patrons, the company is selling cheap, genuine men's and women's wool socks at a loss. Buyers are crowding in, and many are disappointed. In order to make them more accessible, the company is continuing to make great sacrifices, selling 500 dozen women's long genuine wool socks and 300 dozen men's mid-length genuine wool socks, with the price remaining at one dollar and two dimes per two pairs. This price is indeed only one-third of the original price.

The Zhongxi Pharmacy on Sima Road announced that the current grand sale and free gift event has been extremely well received by all sectors. Due to the vastness of Shanghai and the large number of merchants, many have been disappointed. Therefore, the event has been extended for five days, until November 29, to make it more widespread, and thousands of additional valuable prizes and exquisite cosmetics have been added to reward patrons.

The Tongchang Motor Company on Nanjing Road announced that it will hold a 33rd-anniversary grand sale starting tomorrow. In order to increase customer interest, the company will offer discounts ranging from 50% to 10%, and will use a lottery system to refund foreign currency. After the expiration date, an impartial person will draw a day from the discount period, and the company will return the full amount of cash from that day, based on the invoice, in the original foreign currency. If the business income on that day is 10,000 yuan, the company will completely sacrifice 10,000 yuan. This grand event is truly good news for those purchasing vehicles.

Theater News 210

The Xinxin Film Company announced that the company was founded by film giants Zhang Dingwu, Zhou Qimin, and Zhou Minsheng, with a capital of 10,000 yuan, and has established an office in Huayuanfang, Jinshenfu Road. Preparations are now complete, and filming will begin soon. Their debut work is a great social film with a moral message, with martial arts, love, adventure, and gimmicks as its foundation. They are currently working hard to produce costumes, props, and the like.

The Oriental Magic Troupe announced that the troupe's performances are all extremely novel, and all magic equipment, costumes, and scenery are artistically designed, with a capital of approximately 7,000 yuan. They are currently rehearsing and will perform soon.

Page 28

The Fudan Film Company announced that it has been actively rushing to produce the sixth and seventh episodes of "Burning the Seven-Star Tower," and all departments are extremely busy, as never before. Because film merchants in Fujian and Taiwan believe that the "Seven-Star Tower" films are of the highest quality, they sent people yesterday to order ten episodes and agreed on a delivery date, so they must work day and night to rush production. The shooting location has a well-built bandit den, and the scenery is majestic and unparalleled, comparable only to the street scene mentioned the day before. The male lead, Luo Kepeng, is known for his heroic demeanor, and under the careful guidance of director Yu Boyan, his performance has improved rapidly.

The Meiyou Music and Dance Club announced that the club was founded by Zhou Zhibin, Song Yinqian, Gu Shiqing, Yan Yongchang, and Lou Xueying, Min Qixia, Zhang Wanfen, the Fan sisters, and other ladies. It currently has more than 20 male and female members and has set up a preparation office at No. 7 Haiyuanfang, Xibaoxing Road, Zhabei.

The Guanghua Grand Theater at the intersection of Avenue Edward VII and Route Meng-Na-La announced that it premiered the "Four Heavenly Kings" giant film yesterday. Before each performance, the seats were sold out one hour in advance, and the number of spectators was estimated to be no less than 3,000. The situation was extremely crowded, which was the first record broken since the theater opened. From this, one can see the value of the film.
